Legislative Yuan Meeting Passes Law on Traditional Chinese Medicine

(Nanjing) The full text of the Law on Traditional Chinese Medicine, passed by the Legislative Yuan at its 43rd meeting on the 15th, is as follows:

Article 1: Before the examination for Traditional Chinese Medicine practitioners is held by the Examination Yuan, any person who is at least 25 years old and possesses one of the following qualifications, upon passing an examination by the Ministry of Interior and receiving a certificate, may practice Traditional Chinese Medicine: (1) Those who have passed the Traditional Chinese Medicine examination or assessment conducted by the central or provincial government and obtained a certificate; (2) Those who have been issued a medical practice license by the central or provincial government; (3) Those who have graduated from a Traditional Chinese Medicine school and obtained a certificate; (4) Those who have practiced Traditional Chinese Medicine for more than five years. The regulations for the aforementioned examination shall be determined by the Ministry of Interior.

Article 2: Any Traditional Chinese Medicine practitioner currently practicing may continue to practice temporarily before being examined by the Ministry of Interior.

Article 3: Any Traditional Chinese Medicine practitioner who has passed the examination and wishes to practice in a certain place shall present their certificate to the local government in charge and request registration.

Article 4: A Traditional Chinese Medicine practitioner must personally examine a patient before administering treatment and providing prescriptions or issuing diagnostic reports. A Traditional Chinese Medicine practitioner must personally examine a corpse before issuing a death certificate or stillbirth certificate. The formats for the aforementioned death certificate and stillbirth certificate shall be determined by the Ministry of Interior.

Article 5: When a Traditional Chinese Medicine practitioner diagnoses a patient with an infectious disease or examines the corpse of a person who died of an infectious disease, they shall provide instructions on disinfection methods and shall report the facts to the local government or self-governing organization in charge.

Article 6: Traditional Chinese Medicine practitioners have the obligation to accept entrustment and provide assistance from the court, public security bureau, and other administrative government agencies or self-governing organizations in charge regarding matters of adjudication, public safety, and disease prevention.

Article 7: Articles 4, 6, 7, 10, 11, 13, 15, and 17 of the Law on Western Medicine practitioners shall apply mutatis mutandis to Traditional Chinese Medicine practitioners.

Article 8: A Traditional Chinese Medicine practitioner who has been suspended from practice and continues to practice without authorization may be fined up to one hundred yuan by the local government in charge.

Article 9: If a Traditional Chinese Medicine practitioner violates the provisions of this law, unless a sanction has already been determined, the local government in charge may impose a fine of up to fifty yuan. If the violation of the law involves a criminal offense, it shall be handed over to the court for handling.

Article 10: This law shall take effect from the date of promulgation. (Central News Agency dispatch, 15th)

Reports of Victories in Jiangxi and Hubei Bandit Suppression; Rumors of Luo Binghui's Death

(Hankou) According to a telegram from Nanchang to the highest military authorities, all routes in the bandit suppression campaign in Jiangxi have achieved major victories. (Special dispatch, 15th)

(Hankou) Zhang Fang telegraphed that he had routed Ma Xiyou's bandits in Nanyang on the 13th. The bandits retreated to Dahetun, Jianlingdian. (Special dispatch, 15th)

(Hankou) The troops stationed in Henan, Hubei, and Anhui recently suppressed the remaining bandits and seized approximately 3,000 guns. Chiang has issued orders for commendations. (Special dispatch, 15th)

The National Army in Fuzhou achieved a great victory on the front lines in Jiangxi. Chairman Chiang personally commanded the National Army at the front in Nancheng, and after three days of bitter fighting, there was such a great victory. Luo Binghui, the most famous commander-in-chief of the Communist First Army, has already been killed. The National Army has occupied Zixi County. More than 5,000 bandits were killed. On the morning of December 11, the bandit First Army attacked the National Army 90th Division from the south of Yihuang and the west of Guangchang. After a night of fierce fighting, the National Army cut the bandit army into two sections. 800 soldiers in Luo Binghui's bandit army died. As a result, the remaining bandits led their own remnants to surrender to the National Army to show their sincerity. On the 12th of this month, the bandit Third and Fifth Armies, numbering about six brigades, attacked the National Army Fifth, Sixth, and Ninety-Sixth Brigades south of Lichuan. After a day and night of fierce fighting, the bandit army was completely defeated and fled towards Taining. The National Army pursued them and took Dongshan without any effort. In this battle, more than 2,000 bandits were killed. On December 13, the National Army won the final victory. In the past two days, the National Army Fourth and Seventy-Ninth Brigades defeated the bandit Seventh Army, which was the most important militarily, in Zixi County. They occupied the city that evening. Zixi County is the most important base of the bandit army. It is of utmost military importance because it is located on the border of Jiangxi and Zhejiang, with a direct route to Fujian. Around December 14, information was received from the front that Deshengguan (20 li south of Dongshan), which is also of military importance, was occupied by the National Army this afternoon. In these three days, the National Army lost only a small number, a total of just under 400 killed or wounded. The bandit army left behind countless military supplies with each defeat. Military experts believe that in the first three days of battle, the bandit army outnumbered the National Army many times, but they were completely defeated. This was entirely due to Chairman Chiang personally commanding at the front, so the National Army had the courage to kill the enemy. The bandits, after being severely damaged by the National Army this time, are already crestfallen and demoralized, because they know that the final outcome is inevitable. According to the latest report, in the first three days of the battle, the number of wounded bandits was more than twice that of the National Army, estimated to be over 10,000. (National News Agency dispatch, 15th)

Because they were outnumbered, two Japanese soldiers and five passengers were killed, and a total of eight people, including Japanese soldiers, were wounded. Upon receiving an urgent report, Ang'angxi urgently dispatched an armored train. It should be able to recover the route tonight. (Dentsu dispatch, 15th)

The attack by righteous soldiers on the international train at Suhai Station in Qiqihar has been detailed in the previous telegram. According to Sergeant Matsuda of the cavalry unit riding on the train, the attacking righteous soldiers numbered about 350, and it seemed that Russians were in command. They shouted "Kill all Japanese." When the train overturned, gunfire began from both sides of the train, and looting continued until 5:00 AM on the 15th. Later, some righteous soldiers retreated to the west, while the main force retreated towards Jingxing County. The righteous soldiers were also carrying automatic pistols and two machine guns each. (Dentsu dispatch, 15th)

(Harbin) It is learned that in the train robbery case, one Russian, six Chinese, and three Japanese were injured, all civilians. Also injured were three Japanese soldiers, one Russian civilian, one Chinese civilian, and three Chinese soldiers were kidnapped. One employee of the Czech Skoda arms factory is said to have been killed, but this has not been confirmed. Several Japanese are also missing. (Reuters dispatch, 15th)

(Harbin) Last midnight, 300 bandits demolished railway tracks and piled up heavy objects near Tugojia (transliteration), 45 miles west of Qiqihar, causing the eastbound international train to derail and overturn when it arrived there. Then, the bandits opened fire on the train. The small number of guards in the train were unable to resist. The bandits then searched and looted the first and second class carriages, and kidnapped many passengers. It has now been determined that seven passengers were killed and eight were injured. It is still unknown how many injured people have not been found in the broken carriages. At 3:00 AM this morning, Qiqihar sent a Japanese armored train to pursue the bandits and rescue the kidnapped people. There were no British or American passengers in the train. The weather is extremely cold, with a temperature of 50 degrees below zero. (Reuters dispatch, 15th)

Russia Protests to Puppet Regime for Unilaterally Changing Director of Chinese Eastern Railway

(Moscow) According to news from Boli, the Russian Consul General in Harbin, Slavutsky, has protested because the puppet Manchukuo appointed a Manchu as the director of the Chinese Eastern Railway, stating that according to the current treaty, the director must be a Soviet Russian. At the same time, Soviet Russian director Rudy demanded that the puppet Manchukuo police release several detained Soviet Russians and demanded that they stop interfering with the work of Soviet Russian employees of the railway. (National News Agency dispatch, 15th)

The Disarmament Problem: A Touchstone for the League of Nations; British Organizations Hold Rallies in Support; Lord Robert Cecil and Lord Allen of Hurtwood Both Attend and Speak; Resolution Passed Requiring Government to Draft a Plan; Weapons Forbidden to Germany Should Be Abolished by All Countries Equally

(London) The Federation of Organizations Supporting the League of Nations held a general meeting this morning, chaired by Viscount Cecil of Chelwood. Lord Allen of Hurtwood, Secretary-General of the League of Nations Union, also attended. Both Allen and Under-Secretary of State for Foreign Affairs Eden spoke successively, expressing confidence in the mission and future of the League of Nations. Allen said briefly, "If the League of Nations has the support of British public opinion, we will never be disappointed in its fate." Then Viscount Cecil spoke, saying that he did not believe there was a real danger of war, but when he spoke of the policies pursued by the German government, he found the country's expressions of maintaining peace and justice questionable. Cecil said, "We must make disarmament a success, because the disarmament problem is a touchstone for the success or failure of the League of Nations. Although countries are currently engaged in diplomatic negotiations on this matter, if concrete proposals are not put forward as a basis for discussion, I am afraid that the negotiations will not have any effect." Cecil wants the British government to put forward proposals based on the following points: (1) All weapons that the peace treaty prohibits Germany from possessing should be abolished by other countries within five years. (2) International supervision of armaments; (3) Re-stating the obligations of mutual assistance between countries, with economic sanctions imposed for violations of obligations; (4) International supervision of civil aviation; (5) Creation of an international air force, etc. Finally, the conference passed two resolutions. The first resolution expressed confidence in the League of Nations to avoid war. The second resolution required the British government to draft a plan stipulating three points: (1) All weapons that the peace treaty prohibits Germany from possessing should be abolished by all other countries within a certain period; (2) Limiting military expenditures; (3) Implementing phased reductions in armaments under international supervision. (Havas dispatch, 14th)

(London) The Federation of Organizations Supporting the League of Nations held a movement to support the League of Nations. Viscount Cecil of Chelwood and others have given speeches on maintaining the League of Nations. Wickham Steed, the former editor-in-chief of The Times, also recently made a speech in support of this movement. He said, "The League of Nations is the only good organization left over from the European War, and some countries are joining forces to attack it, which is something we cannot condone. If such a large change in the feelings of the general public occurs in these countries, what kind of impact it will have politically cannot be known." Steed also said that once something happens, the people of Germany who have been trained and armed can immediately mobilize millions of people to fight. If we allow them to rearm, the danger would be unthinkable. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

British Ambassadors to France and Germany Return Home to Report on Negotiations

(London) British Ambassador to France, Sir George Clerk, recently returned to London to communicate the British government's views on disarmament and other League of Nations matters. British Ambassador to Germany, Sir Eric Phipps, also came to London for this matter. After arriving this afternoon, he went to the Foreign Office for a long talk with Foreign Secretary Simon. (Reuters dispatch, 14th)

(London) American Ambassador to Germany, Frederic Sackett, returned here this afternoon. According to reports, Sackett has recently met with German Chancellor Hitler many times. The main points of their conversations have been seen in diplomatic reports. Sackett's return home is only to report the details of the conversations to the Prime Minister and Foreign Secretary. (Havas dispatch, 14th)

Foreign Secretary Simon to Travel in Europe During Christmas Holiday

(London) Simon will travel abroad during the Christmas holiday, partly for official business and partly for pleasure. He will first go to Paris, then to Rome, to discuss important matters, and will return to London around January 7 to participate in the work of the Foreign Office, and then go to Geneva to attend the League of Nations Administrative Council meeting on January 15. (Reuters dispatch, 14th)

Rome Expresses Welcome, Showing Favor Toward Germany

Several British newspapers in Rome reported that British Foreign Secretary Simon will travel here during Christmas. Although this news has not been confirmed, those who heard it expressed great welcome. As a result of close contact between the Italian government and the British government, the British attitude towards the disarmament problem has changed. Italy still advocates allowing Germany to increase its military quota to 300,000 men. As for the British proposition, it only wants to prevent Germany from engaging in naval construction. (Havas dispatch, 14th)

Two Ways to Resolve: France and Germany Conclude Non-Aggression Pact, or Adopt British Plan

(London) A few days before Foreign Secretary Simon's trip to the continent, The Times published an opinion stating that there are only two ways to resolve the current difficult international situation: (1) France and Germany conclude a non-aggression pact; (2) Adopt the main principles of the British disarmament plan proposed in March of this year. The newspaper's view on the first point is particularly clear. It said, "If we advocate that France and Germany conclude a non-aggression pact, some people will doubt whether a non-aggression pact is sufficient to guarantee peace. If that were the case, the countries of Europe should have been able to rest easy long ago, because most of the countries have already concluded such treaties. In addition, there are more important treaties, such as the League of Nations Covenant, the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and the Locarno Treaty, which are not included." We have no shortage of words to answer this skeptical argument. It must be known that the reason why European warfare has not broken out until now is largely due to the restrictions imposed by these treaties. This is one. Secondly, German Chancellor Hitler is a revolutionary who has swept away all previous things. As a person, he respects his promises. Since he has formally declared that he will not fight France, this one sentence is enough to reconcile the feelings of the two nations. At present, the biggest obstacle to the conclusion of a disarmament convention lies in the disagreement between France and Germany. If it can be reconciled, there is no fear that the disarmament problem cannot be solved. The Times also said that the final resolution should still be sought in Geneva, but the reconciliation between France and Germany is the key to the solution. The newspaper has always believed that the demands put forward by the German government are not enough to hinder the success of the British disarmament plan, saying that if we establish a general disarmament convention based on the British plan, we can still achieve the goal. As for the potential of a certain country's people to fight, it is not enough to worry about, because if countries universally adopt a short-term military service system, this potential will lose its importance. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

French and Czech Foreign Ministers' Conversations Strictly Confidential

(Paris) This afternoon, Czech Foreign Minister Beneš and French Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour held talks from 5:00 PM to 6:30 PM. Czech Envoy to France Osuský was also present. Beneš declared to the press, "The content of the talks is confidential and cannot be published. We reviewed various issues related to the general policies of the two countries. We will continue the talks tomorrow afternoon. That is all I can tell you." At 6:30 PM, Premier Daladier received Beneš and had a general discussion on the international political situation, with particular emphasis on issues related to the Czech and French sides. Paul-Boncour is scheduled to meet with Beneš again tomorrow afternoon. It is not known whether a third talk will be held, given the importance of the issues discussed by the two foreign ministers. The matters discussed by the two foreign ministers were (1) the League of Nations and the plan to reform the League; (2) the Disarmament Conference and Germany's demands regarding armaments; (3) the organization plan of the countries of Central Europe and the Danube River Basin, etc. A formal communique will be issued after the talks are concluded. Beneš is scheduled to leave France on Monday next week. (Havas dispatch, 14th)

Italian Undersecretary Unexpectedly Leaves Berlin; Opinions Harmonious with German Authorities

(Berlin) Italian Undersecretary for Foreign Affairs Suvich came here on the 12th and contacted various dignitaries. He set off for Cologne tonight. Severe Cold Spreads in London and New York

(London) The temperature in Scotland is between 35 and 40 degrees, but England, Wales, and the European continent are mostly in Arctic climates. The temperature in London today is lower than yesterday. There is ice skating in Windsor Great Park, and the River Avon is frozen in Bath, which has not happened in 30 years. The northeast wind has gradually subsided. The waves in the English Channel are still dangerous. Disaster reports are frequently reported on land and sea. The eastern United States is still cold today, with snowy weather. There is a blizzard in New York. (Reuters dispatch, 14th)

British Aircraft Manufacturing Industry Still Leads the World

(London) According to a certain magazine, in 1933, Britain still held the top position in the world for aircraft materials and aircraft exports. Among all the aircraft in the world, only those manufactured in Britain could operate independently without subsidies. In 1933, British commercial aircraft flew a total of 2,090,000 miles, carrying 56,683 passengers. This compared to 1,604,000 miles and 25,211 passengers in 1931, clearly demonstrating the progress of British aviation in recent years. As for military aircraft, efforts are being made to achieve higher performance, and the current manufacturing trend pays close attention to bombers. (Reuters dispatch, 15th)

Unsinkable Speedboat: Indestructible by Aircraft Bombing; Satisfactory Trial Results

(London) The Daily Telegraph reported today that the first demonstration of an unsinkable speedboat speeding in the North Sea, being attacked by bomber aircraft, was held. The boat was 40 feet long and reached a speed of 30 miles per hour. The aircraft pursued and attacked it, demonstrating amazing skill. Each boat carried three sailors, wearing earmuffs, steel helmets, and gas masks, with minimal other clothing. They lay under unbreakable shelters, steering the boat at high speed, while the aircraft dropped bombs from an altitude of 1,500 feet. Sometimes the bombs hit directly, but the shelters remained intact. The only problem was that fragments from the bombs would hit unprotected wooden parts, penetrating through. In such cases, the sailors had to swim to plug the holes. This trial has been conducted secretly for over a year. (Reuters dispatch, 15th)

A Story of the Occupation of Honolulu: Preface by a Naval Officer; Japanese Ship Carries Propaganda to America; Though a Novel, it Predicts a US-Japan War

Honolulu. After confiscating Japanese propaganda booklets on the ship Chichibu Maru yesterday, important discoveries were made in the booklets today. The book is indeed a novel, but describes in detail the situation when Japan occupied Honolulu during the US-Japan war in 1936. It also has prefaces by senior Japanese naval officers. For example, Admiral Kato, former Commander-in-Chief of the Navy, wrote one of the prefaces, strongly advocating the necessity of Japan's air defense development. In another preface, Vice Admiral Suematsu, the current Commander-in-Chief of the Japanese Combined Fleet, stated that although he could not formally comment on the contents of the booklet, if the Japanese army could achieve victory as described, it would be a great pleasure, and offered congratulations to the author. The narrated wartime events began with a dispute between US and Japanese sailors in Shanghai, followed by Japanese warships sinking the flagship Houston of the US Asiatic Fleet outside Wusongkou. Finally, the US aircraft carriers Lexington and Saratoga, along with a large number of aircraft, were defeated by Japanese aircraft, resulting in a complete Japanese victory. The entire book uses the real names of US and Japanese warships and senior officers. (National Telegram, 14th)

US Marine Corps: Centralized Management Plan; East and West Coast Expeditionary Forces to Merge; Aiming to Save Expenses and Increase Efficiency

(Washington) The Navy Department announced today a plan to reorganize the US Marine Corps, centralizing management to save expenses and increase efficiency. The biggest change is the cancellation of the East and West Coast expeditionary forces, merging them into one, called the Fleet Marine Force. The headquarters will be located in Quantico, Virginia, which currently has approximately 1,000 personnel stationed there, commanded by Lehman. A small team will also be stationed in San Diego, California. In the future, the number of troops stationed in Quantico will increase to 3,500, and San Diego will increase to 1,200. This is the result of a detailed investigation of the Marine Corps in recent months. (National Telegram, 14th)

(Washington) Today, US Army Chief of Staff Dunn announced the purchase of 7,776 vehicles for ten million dollars, for the purpose of "motorizing" the army. The US Army Department has been planning for motorization for several years, and it was gradually implemented last year for testing. (National Telegram, 14th)

US War Debt Due; Only Finland Pays in Full; France, Belgium, and Poland Pay Nothing

(Washington) The State Department announced today that only Finland paid the full amount of the US war debt due tomorrow. Finland is also the only country that has never defaulted. The principal and interest owed by the eleven countries due this time totaled $152,952,637, of which only $8,898,123 was received. (National Telegram, 14th)

(London) The British war debt due to the US amounts to 11,670,000 dollars. The British government has decided to pay 7,500,000 dollars to the US Treasury tomorrow as a sign of sincerity in repaying the debt, pending a final resolution of the war debt issue. This amount will be paid in dollars at the market price. (Havas dispatch, 14th)

(Paris) The French and Belgian governments recently notified the United States by memorandum that they would be unable to pay the war debt due on the 15th of this month. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

Poland: Will Amend the Constitution; Expand Presidential Powers; Eliminate the Party System

Warsaw. The parliamentary club of the Polish government party announced today that it would submit a constitutional amendment to Congress, reducing Congress to an advisory body and concentrating dictatorial power in the hands of the President. Only the President would have the power to appoint and dismiss cabinet members. The reason given was that Poland, dealing with the non-parliamentary governments of Germany and Russia, could no longer retain a democratic system, and that the party system should be eliminated and all power concentrated in the President. World News Agency, London. This is far more beneficial than to nourish me with withered flowers after my death. Any amount, large or small, will be gratefully received. Feltham, Straton Hotel."

White House Statement: Dollar Devaluation Policy Unchanged; Overseas Gold Purchases to Continue; Pound-Dollar Stabilization Still Distant; Speaker of the House Advocates Free Silver Coinage to Avoid Inflation; Treasury Secretary Woodin Denies Resigning This Year

(Washington) The White House issued a statement today declaring that the government does not intend to change its monetary policy. This move by the US President indicates that the US government will resume the process of lowering the value of the dollar as soon as possible, with the apparent goal of devaluing the dollar to fifty cents. However, the White House statement did not mention any specific plans for implementing this process. According to President's Secretary Early, gold purchases will soon be resumed. This White House statement is the result of a two-hour meeting this morning between the President and his closest monetary advisors. It guarantees that the United States will not return to the gold standard for the time being, nor has it been in contact with foreign governments to stabilize the dollar. Although Acting Treasury Secretary Morgenthau firmly denied this morning the rumor that the Federal Reserve Bank had reached an agreement with the central banks of Britain and France to stabilize the dollar exchange rate based on the current gold purchase price of $34.01 per ounce, the rumor persisted for a while. Therefore, the White House issued this statement. Before Secretary Early issued the statement, many non-official observers in this area told reporters that they did not believe the government intended to issue irredeemable "greenback" banknotes, but expected the dollar to continue to devalue, possibly to a lower level by early next spring, after which thoroughly sound "gold certificate" banknotes would be issued with adequate reserves as a guarantee to increase currency. In addition, when Early made the statement, Jones, General Manager of the Reconstruction Finance Corporation, also announced that the company had purchased 446,000 ounces of newly mined domestic gold to date, and had also allocated 526,000,000 yuan to closed and unopened banks. The purchase of bank stocks has also been progressing rapidly recently, with preferred stock and capital notes of 942 banks purchased to date, amounting to 5,300,000,000 yuan. In addition, the silver movement has also made considerable progress. Today, House Speaker Rainey also told reporters that he supported the establishment of a silver bill after the reopening of Congress, and supported the adoption of bimetallism, but based on a ratio of twenty to one. He said that the words of former Democratic presidential candidate Bryan, that there would be no economic panic and decline when the US currency used both gold and silver as its standard, were an irrefutable truth. (National Telegram, 14th)

(Washington) Speaker of the House Rainey told the press that he supported the free coinage of silver, saying that if President Roosevelt proposed such a bill, the House would pass it immediately. "The gold standard we have previously followed will never be seen again in the world." Rainey advocated the re-coinage of silver at a ratio of twenty to one, in order to prevent inflation, saying that if this were done, half of the world would adopt an inflation policy. (Havas dispatch, 14th)

Treasury Secretary Woodin today denied reports that he was planning to resign at the end of the year. Woodin is currently on leave for health reasons, and the department is currently being managed by Acting Secretary Morgenthau. (National Telegram, 14th)

The tax rate for foreign rice is 1.00 gold unit per dan, grain is 0.50 gold unit per dan, the import tax rate for wheat is 0.30 gold unit per dan, and flour is 0.75 gold unit per dan. Barley, buckwheat, corn, and other miscellaneous grains are all taxed at 10% ad valorem. Southwestern Political Affairs Council Establishes Foreign Affairs Discussion Group

Guangzhou Dispatch: The Southwestern Political Affairs Council, in light of increasingly complex foreign affairs issues and the unpredictable international political situation, has established a Southwestern Foreign Affairs Discussion Committee to study the international situation. Multiple foreign affairs experts have been appointed as members to facilitate joint research and discussion. The regulations for the committee's organization have already been formulated, and are excerpted as follows:

Article 1: The Southwestern Political Affairs Council establishes a Foreign Affairs Discussion Committee to research and discuss international and foreign affairs issues.

Article 2: The results of the research and discussions of the matters in the preceding article by this committee shall be submitted to the Southwestern Political Affairs Council for review and approval.

Article 3: This committee shall have several members, three to five of whom shall be standing committee members, and shall designate one standing committee member as chairman. The members of the committee and the standing committee members shall be appointed by the Southwestern Political Affairs Council.

Article 4: This committee shall have three specialized committee members, three section chiefs, and a number of section staff, who shall be appointed by the Southwestern Political Affairs Council.

Article 5: The chairman and the standing committee members shall handle all routine affairs of this committee and act externally in the name of the chairman.

Article 6: The chairman or a committee member shall preside over the meetings of this committee. If the chairman is unable to attend due to circumstances, a standing committee member shall act as chairman. Specialized committee members may attend meetings as non-voting members.

Article 7: This committee shall have the following three sections, with their respective responsibilities as follows: Section 1: Matters related to publicity; Section 2: Matters related to compiling investigation and statistics; Section 3: Matters related to treaties and foreign policy research.

Article 8: This committee may employ staff as deemed appropriate for its operational needs.

Article 9: Detailed operating rules and meeting rules of this committee shall be determined separately.

Article 10: These regulations of this committee shall take effect from the date of promulgation. (December 8)

Jiangxi Province Divided into Eight Blockhouse Zones, Blockade Policy Aims to Annihilate Communists, Constructing Blockhouses to Prevent Communist Movement

Nanchang Dispatch: Chairman Chiang attaches the greatest importance to two aspects of the fifth encirclement and suppression plan: constructing blockhouses to prevent Communist movement and blockading Communist-controlled areas. Before the Fujian Incident, all five provinces, except for eastern Hubei with Huangma as its center, regarded the Jiangxi pseudo-First Front Army as the blockade center. The General Headquarters statistics show that over one hundred counties are involved in the blockade. In this province, except for Ningdu, Xingguo, Yudu, Huichang, Shicheng, Guangchang, Yongxin, Hengfeng, and other counties completely occupied by the Communists, and the provincial capital of Jiujiang, blockade organs have been established in all other areas. Kerosene and salt are sold exclusively by the government, and people can only purchase them with permits. Recently, to improve effectiveness, the General Headquarters has also specially assigned one inspector to every two counties. Sun Yongnian and sixteen others have already been announced as inspectors for thirty-two counties including Linchuan. The inspectors for the remaining thirty-plus counties will also be announced shortly. In addition, 104 investigators have been dispatched to various locations to conduct inspections. As for the effectiveness of the blockade, according to reports from various sources and accounts from those who have escaped from Communist-controlled areas, it is indeed sufficient to annihilate the Communists. For example, Guo Shizeng's troops found a notice from the pseudo-Jin'nan Special Zone stating that seventy catties of rice could be exchanged for two catties and four taels of salt. This is the situation in semi-Communist-controlled areas; the situation in fully Communist-controlled areas can be inferred. As the Communist army regards the Nationalist army's blockade policy as a fatal wound, they are making every effort to break it. In addition to secretly infiltrating safe zones to plunder supplies from time to time, they are also using guerrilla tactics to advance and expand along the borders of the Communist-controlled areas towards non-Communist-controlled areas, appearing and disappearing unpredictably, causing great disturbance. Therefore, in addition to the blockade, the power of blockhouses is also needed to prevent their movement. The General Headquarters has divided the Jiangxi area into eight blockhouse zones, each zone with a supervisory commissioner. The commissioners for the first zone is Li Peigang, (2) Liu Yingfu, (3) Li Genyun, (4) Lin Guoguang, (5) Ji Kanyi, (6) Xu Shengyu, (7) Han Deyuan, (8) Yang Quanjing. At the same time, Chiang has also designated over twenty counties including Linchuan in eastern Jiangxi as blockhouse cluster zones. Blockhouses are being constructed around county towns, market towns, and villages. All bridges on roads open to traffic are also being constructed in the same way. The garrison troops are responsible for defending sections to prevent the Communists from destroying transportation. (December 13)

Promoting Rural Utilization and Cooperation in Recovered Areas, Rescuing Rural Finance, Restoring Farmers' Livelihoods

Nanchang Dispatch: Chairman Chiang, in order to quickly restore farmers' livelihoods in the recovered areas of the provinces suppressing bandits, now that the cleansing of the countryside has already begun, has ordered the establishment of utilization cooperatives to handle lending, sub-lending, and land management. All regulations have been formulated and ordered to be effectively implemented in the provinces suppressing bandits. The main measures are: (1) Lending working capital to members, managing members' land, procuring farming and daily necessities, and buying and selling various goods, to achieve the goal of everyone being able to make a living. The original order is as follows: "After the cleansing of the countryside work begins in the recovered counties and districts of the provinces suppressing bandits, rural finance should be immediately rescued and farmers' livelihoods restored, so that the people can live happily and the source of the bandits can be cut off, achieving permanent peace and laying the foundation for the revival of the localities. For this measure, the General Headquarters of the Three Provinces Suppressing Bandits in Henan, Hubei, and Anhui previously formulated and promulgated the Emergency Rural Financial Relief Regulations for Provinces in Bandit Suppression Areas, and the Regulations for Rural Cooperative Preparatory Societies, etc., and ordered them to be implemented. Now, the original Regulations for Rural Cooperative Preparatory Societies in Bandit Suppression Areas are designed exclusively as preparatory work for reorganizing credit cooperatives. Based on years of experience, since the beginning of the recovery of bandit areas, the problems of rural land ownership and tenancy have been quite prominent, requiring unified control and regulation. Because the recovered counties and districts have long been under Communist influence, land has already been affected by land distribution, and class consciousness is particularly evident in tenancy. Now, at the beginning of pacification, all aspects of land distribution and management, changes in tenancy relations, replenishment of farming tools, and all necessary equipment for farming and life must be brought into the cooperative framework to break the old habit of individuals seeking their own livelihood and seek rapid and effective development. Therefore, the organizational form of the cooperative preparatory societies needed in the recovered counties and districts, in addition to credit cooperatives, should also promote utilization cooperatives, so that in addition to handling lending and sub-lending matters, they can also manage land, integrate landowners and tenants, and jointly seek development. In places where rural revitalization committees have not been established in townships and towns, utilization cooperative preparatory societies can also be used to handle various matters prescribed by the land disposal regulations of those townships and towns, so as to coordinate with the situation and avoid delays. Based on this purpose, a simple version of the Rural Utilization Cooperative Preparatory Society is specifically supplemented in plain language and issued along with this order. Hereafter, in all counties within your jurisdiction that have been designated to apply the Emergency Rural Financial Relief Regulations, in addition to handling rural cooperative preparatory societies, utilization cooperative preparatory societies may also be handled in accordance with the newly issued simplified regulations. You must comply with this and forward it to your subordinates for unified compliance. This order." (December 14)

Tianjin Telephone Bureau Raises Rates, Citing Extremely Difficult Finances and the Need to Pay Interest on Japanese Debt

Tianjin Dispatch: The Tianjin Telephone Bureau has recently sent notices to users informing them that rates will be increased starting January 1 of next year. Businessmen generally believe that at a time when the market is sluggish and business is slow, merchants can hardly bear the increased burden, and are currently planning to oppose it. However, according to the Telephone Bureau, there is a compelling reason for this: In 1926, due to the many inconveniences of manual switchboards, an automatic telephone switchboard was ordered from Siemens in Germany, and a loan of 3 million yuan was obtained from banks such as the Continental Bank, Yien Yieh Commercial Bank, China South Sea Bank, Banque Franco-Chinoise, etc. After the automatic switchboard came into operation, these banks jointly organized a banking syndicate to collect quarterly rentals as collateral, first deducting the interest on the debt, and then returning the remaining amount to the Telephone Bureau to cover all expenses. In the era of manual switchboards, there were approximately 8,000 lines, managed by the General Bureau, East Bureau, South Bureau, and North Bureau. At that time, the monthly rental for businesses was seven yuan, and the monthly rental for households was six yuan, payable quarterly in advance. Later, the General, East, and South Bureaus were converted to automatic switchboards. Also, due to the line configuration of the automatic switchboards, the East Bureau was changed to the Fourth Bureau, the General Bureau was changed to the Second Bureau, and the South Bureau was changed to the Third Bureau. In addition, because the number of automatic lines was insufficient, it was not possible to universally install them within the General Bureau's range. Those belonging to the General Bureau's manual switchboard were named the Fifth Bureau, and the North Bureau was changed to the Sixth Bureau. After the automatic switchboard was implemented, the monthly rental for businesses was changed to ten yuan, and the monthly rental for households was nine yuan. Manual switchboard businesses and households each paid an additional one yuan per month. The Telephone Bureau's monthly income was approximately 120,000 yuan. The monthly income from Tianjin-Shenyang long-distance calls was approximately 30,000 yuan. After deducting the banking syndicate's monthly interest of over 40,000 yuan and the bureau's expenses of 80,000 to 90,000 yuan, the remaining 20,000 to 30,000 yuan was sufficient for purchasing materials and repair costs. Since the September 18th Incident, the propertied class of the Northeast has flocked to Tianjin, and the number of telephone lines has been in short supply. Therefore, 1,000 surplus automatic switchboards were purchased from the Hankou Telephone Bureau, which was still insufficient. However, since the fall of the Northeast, there has been no income from Tianjin-Shenyang long-distance calls, resulting in an annual loss of no less than 200,000 yuan. The bureau's finances have been quite difficult. Rate increases have been repeatedly proposed, but they have not been implemented due to the two disturbances in Tianjin and the turbulent situation. In addition, with the presence of numerous concessions, although the Telephone Bureau is a purely national business, it is difficult to implement anything without first negotiating and coordinating with the concession authorities. The Telephone Bureau once limited the number of calls as a disguised rate increase, but this was not implemented due to the joint opposition of businesses. Therefore, this time's rate increase was first negotiated and coordinated with the leaders of various businesses, and the agreement of the authorities of various concessions was obtained before it could be resolutely decided to implement it on New Year's Day next year. It is anticipated that there will be some minor disturbances, but the leaders of various businesses will surely be able to persuade and guide, and the authorities of various concessions will surely be able to assist, so it should not be a problem. Upon investigation, for those with automatic switchboards, the rate for households will not be increased (still nine yuan per month). Special businesses such as banks, silver shops, money shops, restaurants, hotels, bathhouses, etc., will be increased by four yuan per month (i.e., fourteen yuan). The remaining are ordinary businesses, which will be increased by one yuan per month (i.e., eleven yuan). For those with manual switchboards, the rate for households will not be increased. Special businesses and ordinary businesses will each be increased by one yuan per month (i.e., eight yuan / nine yuan). In addition, the telephone deposit will be changed to a telephone guarantee deposit: 50 yuan per automatic switchboard (main or extension), and 30 yuan per manual switchboard. There are approximately 8,000 automatic switchboards and approximately 3,000 manual switchboards in the city. This rate increase, excluding households, will increase monthly revenue by approximately ten thousand yuan. If viewed superficially, this increase will slightly alleviate the Telephone Bureau's financial difficulties. In reality, the bureau will not receive any of this money. At a certain time, a certain important person borrowed one million yuan from the China-Japan Industrial Company, with a monthly interest rate of one percent. The contract stated that the Tianjin Telephone Bureau would guarantee it. Later, due to the many troubles of the nation, the principal and interest were not secured. Since the September 18th Incident, the Japanese have revealed their ferocious faces and have become increasingly aggressive in their demands for repayment. They finally declared that if this debt was not repaid, they would send troops to occupy the Telephone Bureau (the Telephone General Bureau is very close to the Japanese concession). The Ministry of Communications was forced to allocate and remit 10,000 yuan per month to the Tianjin Telephone Bureau to repay the interest. Therefore, this rate increase is only enough to pay the interest on the Japanese debt, slightly reducing the burden on the Ministry of Communications, and has nothing to do with the Telephone Bureau. However, the relevant parties are tight-lipped about who borrowed this Japanese debt, when it was borrowed, and what it was used for, which is quite strange. (December 13)

Songjiang Tricycle Kills a Person

The local tricycles were formerly subject to a small licensing fee by the district office to indicate management. Later, the various tricycle businesses, citing the slump in business, successively closed down, ceasing to pay the fees, but continued to rent out tricycles secretly, so that they could be seen everywhere on the streets. Moreover, some unscrupulous people would deliberately crash into women in the street for fun, causing them to panic and avoid them. As a result, accidents would occur from time to time due to unskilled driving. The other night, a resident of Jiuqu Lane, Shen Huizhang, accompanied his sister to watch a talkie movie. Upon reaching the entrance of the Grand Theater, Shen's sister was violently knocked to the ground by a speeding tricycle. She lost consciousness for a moment, and then began deliriously babbling. Shen Huizhang immediately hired a carriage to transport his sister back to Dr. Li Wangping for treatment. She died of her injuries yesterday. The passenger who caused the accident has been arrested by the Second Precinct and transferred for investigation. After this case occurred, it is heard that the authorities will strictly ban the passage of tricycles to ensure the safety of travelers.

Dispute Over Widening of Gong Lane

The Wuxian County Government's widening of Gong Lane and Qianjiangfang Street in the city has been nearing completion since work began. However, the width of the streets, as stipulated by the Department of Construction, is eight meters for the carriageway and two meters for the sidewalks on both sides. Unexpectedly, the contractor in charge has arbitrarily reduced the width, reducing the carriageway to seven meters. As a result, the local people are very dissatisfied. Yesterday (15th), Wang Ligeng and others submitted a petition to the Department of Construction, requesting that it order the reconstruction to widen the streets to eight meters to maintain traffic, and also requested that the county government's supervisory personnel be punished. It is heard that the Department of Construction has already heard about this matter, so when Qian Tianpeng, director of the technical office, went to the province to apply for this funding the day before, there were no good results.

Wuxi Uncovers Drug Pill Operation

Yesterday afternoon, Yao Chunjie, deputy captain of the Public Security Bureau's detective team, acting on a confidential report, stated that there was a secret drug pill manufacturing operation set up by Chen Rengen and others in the workshop of Li Fan's house in Changkang Lane near Hanchang Ridge outside Guangfu Gate. He requested that police be dispatched to search the premises. After receiving the report, Yao immediately dispatched more than ten detectives to Changkang Lane to conduct a search. They arrested the main suspect, Chen Rengen, and three others on the spot, along with the landlord, Li Fan. They also found a large quantity of drug pills, Quick Pill, and heroin, etc., worth about 700 or 800 yuan. They were all taken to the bureau and transferred to the county court for interrogation.

Robbery Occurs in the Urban Area

Chen Anpei, a resident of Yangjian Town, Huaixia City, Eighth District, is in his twenties and comes from a wealthy family. His father, Zhiying, passed away many years ago. His mother, Qiang, is still alive and well. Several years ago, Anpei married a woman named Gong, and they have a son. The family of several people lived a happy life. Several years ago, due to unrest in the countryside, Chen moved to Yingshanhe in the city. This year, he built a building under the Blue Stone Bridge on the embankment in the East Gate and moved in on the second day of the lunar month. Unexpectedly, at about six o'clock in the evening of the 14th, five robbers suddenly came and, after entering the house, two robbers each produced a Mauser pistol, and one robber held a sharp blade, shouting to prevent anyone from making a sound. At that time, Chen's mother, Qiang, in a moment of quick thinking, took advantage of the fact that the robbers were driving the male and female servants into a room and locking them up, sneaking out the door and running wildly towards Huaixiu Bridge in the East Gate, shouting loudly for help. The robbers inside heard the noise and knew that things were not good. Without waiting to rob, three robbers fled in the direction of Huayuan Lane, and two robbers fled in the direction of Yang Hengtai distillery. At this time, the neighbors around had already heard the noise and came out, and seeing the two robbers running wildly, they chased after them together. As a result, one robber was caught on the spot, while the others escaped. Shortly after, Zhou Guangchun, clerk of the East Gate Guard Post, and Hu Wenhua, officer of the Hanxiu Bridge post, arrived at the scene one after another, and escorted the robber to the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau. Commissioner Qin opened the court. The victims, Chen Anpei and Chen Qiang, went to the bureau to prove that the robber was definitely a robber. According to the robber's confession, his name was Liu Weimin, he was 49 years old, and he was from Henan. He had just arrived in Wuxi this morning to visit friends. He denied robbing. Based on the confession, Commissioner Qin believed that since the robber was caught on the spot and identified by the victims, it was inappropriate to allow him to quibble. So he submitted it to the General Public Security Bureau yesterday and transferred it to the County Court for handling.

Zhenjiang Cheng Zhuang Accused Again After Release from Prison

Cheng Zhuang, former district chief of the Fifth Water Police District, and accountant Gao Tong, who had been detained for years, were released on bail after being transferred to the court, and after repeated investigations, it was determined that Cheng et al. had not embezzled anything and were released on bail. Unexpectedly, former patrol officer Hang Yu and others of the Fifth Water Police District separately submitted reports to the Provincial Department of Civil Affairs and the court yesterday, saying that Cheng et al. had been in arrears with the salaries of the official police and other personnel for many days while in office, and had not paid them, and that they had embezzled them for their own benefit. They requested a thorough investigation and ordered them to be paid.

Changshu Teenager Murders Aunt

Gong Pinru, who opened Daheng Xie Silk Shop in Dongtang Town, Third District, married Ni and had two daughters, the eldest named Cuiyuan, who is now twelve years old. Gong's family also includes his old mother and nephew, etc. The nephew is named Xingbao, and is now seventeen years old. His father died eleven years ago. He was usually raised by his grandmother, who loved him very much. He graduated from Dongtang City Primary School and then studied at the Rural Normal School, but dropped out halfway because he was unwilling to endure hardship. However, his aunt strictly disciplined him, and Xingbao hated her deeply. His neighbor, Shao Xinlian, an apprentice at Hengfeng Shun Cloth Shop, is extremely friendly with Xingbao, and their friendship is like brothers. On the 13th of this month, the two secretly agreed to murder their aunt, Ni. On that day, Pinru and his grandmother were not at home. The two drank yellow wine until late at night, and then quietly took a knife and entered their aunt's room. They opened the mosquito net and slashed. At that time, Ni was fast asleep and woke up from her dream. She was struck in the lower back, and a knife was chopped into her right shoulder, and blood flowed freely. Her daughter, Cuiyuan, heard the noise and got up to look, and her nose was also cut off. Seeing that their plan had been achieved, the two teenagers abandoned their knives and went away. Afterwards, five letters were found in Xingbao's room, all addressed to his friends, detailing the process of the murder. The two victims have been sent to the Yuhe Hospital in the city. Their lives are in danger. Their family members are now searching for the whereabouts of the two murderers for investigation.

Yangzhou Zhenyang Automobile Company's Dispute Over Driver Examinations

In order to improve its operations, the Zhenyang Automobile Company specially examined the skills of its drivers on the 13th, so that the better ones could drive small cars. This is because passengers in small cars often reward drivers with a considerable tip in addition to the fare. This extra income is not available when driving large cars. The company originally implemented a method of fairness, whereby all drivers could take turns driving small cars a certain number of times each month, so that all drivers could have extra income. This method has been in place for several years. Recently, the company felt that no one was responsible for the damage and loss of parts on the cars. Whenever the company inquired, everyone would shirk responsibility. Therefore, the company believed that it was necessary to make proper regulations, hence the examination. However, the drivers believed that large cars have a large number of passengers, and their driving responsibility is twice as important as that of small cars. Why should they pay special attention to small cars? Moreover, most of the drivers have been serving for many years, and the company has long known the quality of their skills. The company has the freedom to dispose of it, why do you have to take this step, trampling on the workers? Therefore, the union chairman, Zhou Jinbang, was publicly promoted to represent the refusal to take the exam. The company did not allow it, and Zhou was fired. Upon hearing the news, the union convened a board of supervisors under the guise of the county party department, expressed its dissatisfaction, and discussed the methods to deal with it.

Nantong Kidnapping Ring Leader Sentenced to Death

He Tinggui, the famous kidnapping ring leader in Tonghai, committed numerous crimes. He was arrested by the police and the security forces and sent to the county government for interrogation. He pleaded guilty and has been sentenced to death. His accomplices, Yu Zhoufu and Ding Zikui, have also been arrested by the Public Security Bureau and sent to the court. They have all been tried and sentenced to death.

The Jiaxing County Public Security Bureau received a report stating that Zhang Erbao's house in Jiaoli Street was hiding abducted children with the intention of selling them. They immediately ordered the police to search the house. They arrested Zhang Erbao on the spot and rescued two abducted boys, Pan Zhenbao (20 years old, a road intermediary) and Fei Fuzhen (12 years old, from Chongde). The human trafficker, Tang Youzhen, had already fled after hearing the news, and had taken with him a 15-year-old girl who had been abducted. Zhang Erbao and the two boys, Pan and Fei, have been sent to the court for questioning and handling.

After Zhang Qingze, the county magistrate of Mu County, was dismissed by order, Zhang Zhouwen, the county magistrate of Xiangshan County, was transferred by the province to take over. Yesterday, the new county magistrate came to Ping, bringing more than thirty people with him. He stayed at the Tongan Hotel in Xiaojie. He has scheduled to take over the seal at 3 pm today. Local News: French Minister Arrived in Shanghai from Beijing Yesterday Morning; Sino-French Friendship Association Hosted a Farewell Luncheon Yesterday Afternoon; He Will Return to His Country Today on the Laussac; French Senator Honorat Accompanies Him

After receiving permission from the French government to take leave and return to his country, French Minister to China, Mr. Wilden, immediately went to Beijing from Beiping to bid farewell to Foreign Minister Wang and others of the National Government. He arrived in Shanghai at 7:30 yesterday morning on a night express train from Beijing. Accompanying the French Minister was Mr. Honorat, the former French Minister of Education and current Senator. The French Consul-General in Shanghai, Mr. Meyrier, and Consul Mr. Gauthier, and others went to welcome them. After getting off the train, Mr. Wilden took a car that was waiting for him and went directly to the French Consulate on Rue du Consulat for a rest. All French expatriates in Shanghai held a public banquet at the French Chamber of Commerce yesterday at noon. Chinese committee member Li Shizeng held a grand tea party at Ferguson Road at 6 o'clock yesterday to bid farewell. Last night at 7 o'clock, French Consul-General Meyrier hosted a farewell banquet at the Consulate, and important French military and political figures staying in Shanghai at the time were invited to attend. In order to save time and avoid having to say goodbye to everyone and decline those who wished to see him off at the pier, Mr. Wilden has decided to hold a farewell reception at the French Consulate at 1:30 this afternoon (the 16th). All French expatriates staying in Shanghai and officials from our government can attend at that time. At 3 o'clock in the afternoon, Mr. Wilden, accompanied by his wife and French Senator Honorat, will leave Shanghai on the French mail ship Laussac to return to his country. The Sino-French Friendship Association held a farewell banquet for him at the French Chamber of Commerce on Avenue Mercier at 12:30 yesterday noon. At 6 o'clock last night, three groups, including the World Society, World College, and Sino-French University, held a farewell meeting. The details are recorded separately as follows:

Friendship Association Banquet

The figures present yesterday included Chinese committee members Cai Yuanpei and Li Shizeng, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan Chu Minyi, former Chinese Minister to France Qian Xinzhi, former Chargé d'Affaires to Belgium Xie Shou Kang, President of the Sino-French Friendship Association Wang Jingqi, Secretary Jiang Wenxin, Directors Li Xinyang, Song Wusheng, Wei Yu, French Consul-General Meyrier, Consul Gauthier, French Police Inspector Fabre, Director of the Education Department of the French Municipal Council Colbert, French Chargé d'Affaires Aubaret, President of the French Literary Association Liu Hong, Secretary Lin Jun, President of Aurora University Qian Ermen, and guests Yang Yannian, Hu Guocheng, Hu Wunyao, Nong Ruhui, Ji Zongmeng, Ms. Huang Mingmin, Ms. Wang Ximing, and more than two hundred reporters from Chinese and Western newspapers.

A Glimpse of the Venue

The venue was the French Chamber of Commerce on Avenue Mercier. The French police specially dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to guard the entrance. President of the Sino-French Friendship Association Wang Jingqi, Vice President Colbert, and Secretary Jiang Wenxin, among others, personally acted as hosts. Guests were required to sign in upon arrival. The banquet was held in the large living room on the second floor. French flags were hung on all four walls. The long rectangular table against the wall was for the French Minister and the former French Minister of Education. There were more than ten other circular tables, with the central area reserved for reporters from Chinese and Western newspapers. French Minister Wilden and former French Minister of Education Honorat arrived at the venue around 12 o'clock. Guests entered the venue one after another according to their assigned seats. The venue was solemnly decorated, and the atmosphere was enthusiastic, truly a grand occasion unprecedented.

Mr. Wang's Congratulatory Speech

During the banquet, Mr. Wang Jingqi, President of the Sino-French Friendship Association, delivered a congratulatory speech, stating briefly: "Today, the Sino-French Friendship Association is holding a celebration and luncheon to commemorate its establishment. It is a great honor to have French Minister Wilden, who is taking leave from Shanghai, and former French Minister of Education Honorat, who is passing through Shanghai on his way back to his country, invited to attend. The cultural relationship between China and France has a long history. In order to strengthen the ties between Chinese and French people and facilitate cultural exchange between the two countries, the Sino-French Friendship Association was established. Today, there are more than two hundred members present, making this the Association's first grand gathering. With the presence and guidance of Mr. Cai, Mr. Li, and others, we foresee boundless hope for the future. French Minister Wilden is scheduled to return to his country tomorrow. We wish him a smooth journey and hope that he will return to China soon to preside over the friendship between China and France."

French Minister's Reply

French Minister Wilden then replied, stating briefly: "I am very grateful for today's banquet. I have been in China for thirty-five years. Although I am temporarily returning to my country, I am reluctant to leave China. However, before leaving China, I attended the groundbreaking ceremony for the Sino-French Friendship Association in Nanjing yesterday, and today I am attending the celebration of the establishment of the Sino-French Friendship Association. I find it very interesting. This association is an organization for strengthening Sino-French relations. I hope that China and France will understand each other, be open and honest with each other, and have no secrets, so that we can avoid misunderstandings. I am very willing to do my best to help the Sino-French Friendship Association and promote it in France after I return to my country."

Mr. Honorat's Reply

Next, former French Minister of Education Honorat replied, stating briefly: "I have always been very close to Chinese culture. I co-founded the Sino-French University in Lyon with Mr. Li Shizeng to promote Sino-French cultural exchange. During this visit to China, I saw that the Chinese countryside has vast lands suitable for agricultural products, and its future development is limitless. I am very grateful to be attending this grand gathering today. I wish everyone success."

Public Lecture

At the invitation of the French Literary Association, Mr. Honorat gave a public lecture at 5:30 yesterday afternoon in the grand auditorium of the Association at 11 Rue du Consulat. More than five hundred Chinese and French people attended. The lecture was introduced by Mr. Lihong, President of the French Literary Association. Mr. Honorat is currently the Rector of the University District of Paris. The topic of the lecture was the University District of Paris. A reporter from the Shanghai News Agency has extracted and recorded his speech as follows: Mr. Honorat said that the University District of Paris is a district for university students from all countries. It is a French plan from eight years ago. The preparation has cost 300 million pounds so far. Universities from various countries have already built there. The purpose of building the University District is to gather university students from various countries in one place, so that they can gradually eliminate national concepts, remove boundaries between each other, and seek the assimilation of the world. Therefore, this matter is not a French undertaking, but an international undertaking. France originally only has nationality but no ethnicity, so there is no concept of ethnicity. He hopes that the University District will develop day by day, so that all ethnic groups in the world can cooperate together.

Three Groups Farewell

The World Society, World College, and Sino-French University held a meeting at 6 o'clock yesterday afternoon at the Society on Ferguson Road to bid farewell to French Minister Wilden and French Minister of Education Honorat. French Consul Meyrier, Cai Yuanpei, Zhang Jingjiang, Wu Tiecheng, Chu Minyi, Zhang Xiaolin, Du Yuesheng, Ye Yuhu, Wang Shisun, Wu Yunzhai, Chen Zeqing, and more than two hundred others attended, making it a grand occasion. He also said that Mr. Honorat is the advocate of the cultural city, and he himself will go to Europe soon to discuss the progress of this work with Mr. Honorat to promote the development of cultural cooperation between China and France and between China and the international community. Then, Mr. Wilden and Mr. Honorat expressed their gratitude, praising Mr. Li's dedication to international cultural work and hoping that he would come to France soon. Mr. Li led them on a tour, and at the end, the Datong Music Society performed national music. The guests and hosts enjoyed themselves and dispersed when the clock struck eight.

Returning Home Today

French Minister Wilden is scheduled to leave Shanghai on the French mail ship Laussac with his wife and Mr. Honorat at 3 o'clock this afternoon to return to his country. Mr. Wilden is 57 years old and came to China at the age of 23. He initially worked on the Chinese railway and then became a diplomat. In 1928, he took over as the French Minister to China, and has been in office for five years. He has a very harmonious relationship with China and France. This time, he is taking leave to return to his country for a period of six months, and is expected to come to China to cancel his leave around June next year. During his leave, all ministerial affairs will be temporarily handled by Chargé d'Affaires Aubaret.

Kong Xiangxi Came to Shanghai to Discuss the Ministry of Finance's Rectification of Land Tax; It is Proposed to Submit it at the Fourth Plenary Session; The Imposition of Inheritance Tax is in the Planning Stage

Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi arrived in Shanghai on a night train from Beijing at 7:30 yesterday morning. After getting off the train, he went directly to his private residence on Avenue Petain for a rest. At 11 o'clock, he met with reporters from various newspapers to give a speech. The details are recorded separately as follows:

Ministry of Finance Proposes to Rectify Land Tax

In response to questions from reporters, Mr. Kong first stated that at this Fourth Plenary Session, he will represent the Ministry of Finance with a proposal to rectify land tax. The land tax in various provinces is so complicated that it is difficult to describe. Some have little land but heavy taxes, some have much land but light taxes, and some even have land but no taxes. Since the abolition of Likin, various provinces have lost a source of financial revenue, so they have thought about the people (farmers) and created various names to compensate for the land tax. According to my recent investigation, although the methods of collection in various provinces are different, their purpose of levying is the same. For example, the province levies it, the county levies it, the local levies it, and even the garrison levies it. There are so-called "educational surcharges" and "defense surcharges," etc., with more than thirty kinds of names. Especially in Sichuan, it is heard that land tax has been levied for more than fifty years since the Republic of China. Such layers of harsh levy have led to the bankruptcy of the countryside, and the people are struggling to survive. Farmers work hard all year round, but they cannot even eat their fill, so they take risks, and bandits rise up. Land tax originally falls under the jurisdiction of the Ministry of Finance. In order to eliminate accumulated malpractices and provide relief, so that farmers can breathe a little, I have specially proposed the case of land tax rectification at this plenary session to arouse the attention of all members and discuss rectification methods together.

Reasons for the Postponement of the Fourth Plenary Session

Mr. Kong also said that the Central Committee has dispatched Zhang Ji, Ma Chaojun, Chen Zhaoying, and Wang Luyi to the south. Their task is to urge the members in the southwest to come to Beijing to attend the Fourth Plenary Session. However, the Fourth Plenary Session was originally scheduled to be convened in Beijing on December 20. Now that the meeting date is approaching, the members who went to Guangzhou to urge the southwestern members to come to Beijing have just arrived in Guangdong. It is difficult for the members to arrive in advance, so it has been decided to postpone it for one month so that the members can come to Beijing to attend the meeting at ease. The rumor that the postponement of the Fourth Plenary Session is to wait for the members such as Zhang Ji to return to Beijing to report is not true. As for whether Mr. Hu Zhantang can come to Beijing, there is no news so far.

Opening up Political Power Must Go Through Tutelage

A Hong Kong telegram reported that Chairman Chiang sent a telegram to the southwest, expressing his agreement with the idea of opening up political power. When reporters asked Mr. Kong about this, he said that the "National" in the Kuomintang means the party of the people. Anyone who is a citizen can join. After joining the party, after the period of tutelage, they will have the right to vote and be elected. Before the Kuomintang has thoroughly completed the work of tutelage, for the sake of the country and the nation, it is not allowed to abdicate its responsibility. It must wait until the work of tutelage is completed and the people have the ability to enact a constitution before the period of tutelage can be ended and constitutional government can be implemented. It is not yet time to talk about "opening up political power." If you want to have political power, as long as you do not betray the party's ideology and resolutely follow the teachings of the Premier and join the Kuomintang, you can have political power at any time. Moreover, in the past and present, there are also many non-Kuomintang members who have obtained political power. For example, many ministers and committee members of the government are not Kuomintang members. This can be said that the Kuomintang has never truly implemented the so-called "dictatorship" and has already given political power to people outside the party.

The Imposition of Inheritance Tax is in the Planning Stage

The Ministry of Finance is still planning to collect inheritance tax. As for the import tax on foreign rice and wheat, it has been decided to implement the collection from the 16th. However, Guangdong and Guangxi provinces have always been rice ports, and the people's food depends on foreign rice and wheat. At the same time, the authorities in these provinces have also levied a business tax of one yuan per dan on foreign rice and wheat, so it has been decided to exempt the collection to maintain the people's food. The only purpose of levying import tax on foreign rice and wheat is to protect domestic rice and wheat. Therefore, if in the future a certain province does not have enough rice and wheat to feed its people, then the import tax on foreign rice and wheat should also be exempted to make up for it.

The Continental News reported that Mr. Dier, an American instructor at the Kuanqiao Central Aviation School, was injured in a flight at the Kuanqiao Airport last night (the 14th).
