The National Goods Sports Meeting of the Special Zone Opened Yesterday; Representatives from All Walks of Life Numbered Over 300; A Declaration was Issued to Encourage the Promotion of National Goods; The National Goods Market will Begin Exhibition Today

The Shanghai Special Zone National Goods Sports Meeting, sponsored by the National Goods Manufacturers Association of this city, was held at the Guanghua Theater on Avenue Edward VII and Avenue Foch at 10 o'clock yesterday morning. The exhibition hall and temporary market for national goods manufacturers' products were changed to be opened at the site of the Pudong Fellow Villagers Association at 9 o'clock this morning due to rain and insufficient arrangements. The details are recorded separately as follows:

Representatives Present

The representatives present included Director of the International Trade Bureau He Bingxian, Director of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau Wu Xingya (represented by Wu Hengru), Lin Kanghou of the Bankers Association, Wang Yansong of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Zhang Yichen and Chen Binghui of the First Special Zone Citizens Association, Mao Yun of the Second Special Zone Citizens Association, and representatives from various factories such as Guanshengyuan, Dongya Woolen Mill, and Yabuer Electric Factory, totaling about 300 people.

Chairman's Report

After the ceremonial rites, Cao Zhigong was publicly elected by the presidium to report, stating briefly that the association is holding the opening ceremony today in the wind and rain, and we are grateful to all of you for braving the rain to attend, which shows the enthusiasm of all walks of life for the national goods movement. I would like to thank you on behalf of the association. As for the motivation of the association to hold this event, it is because we feel that the special zone concession is filled with foreign goods, but in the past two years, although there are national goods stores opened in the central area with a relatively large scale, the western area is located in a remote place, and national goods stores are almost non-existent. Therefore, the association specially led employees and factories to hold the national goods sports meeting here, in order to arouse the citizens' deep impression of the national goods movement. We hope that all walks of life and citizens will criticize and purchase as much as possible. We must know that the special zone is subject to the control of the environment and is in a precarious situation, but we must break through all difficulties and see the blue sky and white sun again, so that the national goods movement can achieve the final victory.

Summary of Speeches

After the chairman finished his report, Director of the International Trade Bureau He Bingxian gave a speech, stating briefly that today, China's commerce is declining, and all economic organizations are on the verge of bankruptcy. The main reason is that the number of imports is increasing day by day, and the number of exports is decreasing. At present, the only way to remedy this is for the Chinese people to work hard to promote national goods, for various factories to improve their products, and for the Chinese people to be happy to purchase national goods, then foreign goods will naturally decrease, and perhaps we can recover from this situation. Then, Wu Huanru, the representative of the Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, gave a speech, stating that in recent years, foreign goods have been rampant, and China's markets have been doing their best to dump, which has led to a slump in Chinese commerce. This is one of the reasons for China's poverty. Furthermore, since the loss of the four northeastern provinces, our country's exports have decreased even more, while imports have increased day by day. The amount of leakage is truly shocking. If we do not find a way to remedy this, the future is unimaginable. I have seen the enthusiasm of the Japanese for using national goods and admire it very much. The people are determined not to use foreign goods and to purchase as much domestic goods as possible. I deeply hope that the Chinese people will follow suit. Wang Yansong, Lin Kanghou, and others also gave speeches in succession, with many warnings. The speeches were too long to be recorded in detail.

Declaration

The association issued a declaration stating that the most difficult and unsolvable problem in the world is the economic problem. Since the conclusion of the Treaty of Versailles, the military struggle between countries has temporarily ceased on the surface, and economic competition has emerged. The strength of a country does not lie in the strength of its military force, but in the fullness or emptiness of its national power. Those who have mass production and can be self-sufficient and provide for others will inevitably be strong and rich. Therefore, those in power today pay attention to promoting production, cultivating the foundation of the country, and using dumping policies to build strong tariff barriers in order to seek self-improvement. The economy is related to the country like blood vessels are to the human body. Our country's economic system has always been perfect. A family of eight living in a five-acre house was a beautiful thing in ancient times. Since the opening of the sea ban, the Chinese people have been confused by the novelty of foreign goods and have been buying them one after another. Over the years, it has become a habit, resulting in a daily increase in the import of foreign goods and the outflow of money, which is more than just a million. Taking the past two years as an example, according to the statistics of the International Trade Bureau from January to September, the trade deficit was 2,560,802,814 yuan. The amount of leakage is truly shocking. If this continues, the economy will go bankrupt and the nation will perish. Shanghai is an area for dumping foreign goods. People are accustomed to luxury and value foreign goods, especially in the special zone. In view of this, the association has led its employees and factories to hold this meeting, gathering the essence of national goods from all over the country in one place to meet the world, so that compatriots across the country have the opportunity to recognize national goods. Although the scale is not grand, it has done its best to collect as much as possible. We hope that from now on, people from all walks of life, whenever they need something, will only use national goods, so that production and sales can be integrated into one, and the national economy and people's livelihood will benefit both. This is our declaration.

A Glimpse of Slogans

(1) Promoting national goods is the duty of the people. (2) Promoting national goods is a weapon against insults. (3) Promoting national goods is resisting the enemy. (4) Promoting national goods is realizing the Premier's Principle of People's Livelihood. (5) I am Chinese, I should use Chinese goods. (6) National goods save the country is the Premier's legacy. (7) Use national goods for everything you need for clothing, food, and housing. (8) Using national goods expresses the spirit of the Chinese nation.

All are welcome to visit and purchase as much as possible.

Import Tax on Foreign Rice and Wheat to be Levied from Today; The Result of Past Awards for Imports Was Low Grain Prices and Injured Farmers; Levying Import Tax Opens the First Page of the History of People's Food

According to the Shin Shi News Agency's report from this city, the Ministry of Finance has ordered all customs in the country, except for Guangdong, Guangxi, and Fujian, to levy import tax on foreign rice and wheat, and has decided to start levying it from today. In the past, in order to take care of the people's food, the government adopted a policy of "prohibiting exports and rewarding imports," and there were no taxes on the import of foreign rice and wheat. Now, due to changes in the environment and the needs of reality, we have to change the traditional policy to "opening up exports and restricting imports." The Shin Shi News Agency reporter believes that today is one of the most memorable days for reforming the people's food problem. The levy situation and the past import situation of foreign rice are explored and recorded as follows:

Rice and Wheat Tax Rates

The import tax on foreign rice has been clearly stipulated in the Ministry of Finance's decree yesterday. However, foreign goods are usually subject to an additional tax of one-tenth. This additional tax was originally caused by disaster relief and has been followed to this day and has not been canceled. Imported rice and wheat are also a kind of foreign goods and cannot be an exception. The tax rates of the principal and additional taxes are converted into national currency as follows: (1) Rice: each dan (calculated as 100 catties, equivalent to 605/1000 of the old customs balance, the same below), 1.00 gold unit, plus 1/10 of the additional tax, a total of 1.10 gold unit, equivalent to 1 yuan, 9 jiao, 8 fen, 5 li in national currency. (2) Grain: each dan 0.50 gold unit, plus 1/10 of the additional tax, a total of 0.55 gold unit, equivalent to 1 yuan, 4 fen in national currency. (3) Wheat: each dan 0.30 gold unit, plus 1/10 of the additional tax, a total of 0.33 gold unit, equivalent to 6 jiao, 2 fen, 5 li in national currency. (4) Flour: each dan 0.75 gold unit, plus 1/10 of the additional tax, a total of 0.825 gold unit, equivalent to 1 yuan, 5 jiao, 6 fen, 4 li in national currency. (5) Other miscellaneous grains: in addition to levying an ad valorem tax of 10%, an additional tax of 1/10 must also be added (the price of the gold unit is based on the Central Bank's market price yesterday).

Secret Order from the Ministry of Finance for Implementation

The Ministry of Finance was deeply concerned that the issuance of this tax order would affect the market, so it was implemented by secret order. The matter was very secret beforehand. The Customs Administration and the General Inspectorate of Customs received the secret order on the 10th, and only on the afternoon of the 13th did they jointly send a telegram to the customs across the country (excluding Guangdong, Guangxi, and Fujian), requiring them to start collecting taxes on the 16th (that is, today). At the same time, the Jianghai Customs was notified by telephone to comply. After receiving the telephone order, the Customs completed the Chinese and English announcements within one hour and distributed them to various newspapers for announcement. Therefore, on the 14th, various Chinese and foreign newspapers in this city published the Jianghai Customs' announcement on the collection of import tax on foreign rice and wheat. The Customs Administration also instructed the relevant departments on the 14th to be informed.

Recent Import Statistics

The government has always tried its best to encourage the import of food in order to stabilize domestic market prices. For example, in the third year of the Yongzheng era, Siam was allowed to transport rice to China. In the sixtieth year of the Kangxi era, an edict was issued to Siam to transport rice to Fujian, Guangdong, Ningbo, and other places for sale, and taxes were exempted. During the Qianlong, Jiaqing, and Daoguang eras, there were also similar awards, but there are no statistics on how much was imported, but the amount should not be small. Since the sixth year of the Tongzhi era of the Qing Dynasty, there have been imports every year. According to customs statistics, by August of this year, 413 million dan of foreign rice had been imported in 73 years. The above statistics show that the most was in 1923, about 22.4 million dan. This year may exceed the number of 1923. This huge leak is the result of the awards given by previous generations. If we do not urgently seek remedies, the future is unimaginable.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Telegram to the Central Government

The Flour Mill Association of this city agrees with the rice and wheat tax, but the American wheat that has been ordered for various ships was originally the goods underwritten by the central government, and the goods were ordered in advance, so they cannot bear this heavy tax. In the past two days, continuous meetings have been held at the New Kai River Vocational Association and the Bank Club to discuss remedies. It was decided to request the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to forward a telegram to the central government to exempt the import tax on the American wheat that has been ordered but not yet arrived. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce agreed to send a telegram to the central government, requesting an exemption. The original telegram said: To the Nanjing Executive Yuan, Ministry of Finance, and Customs Administration: According to a letter from the Flour Mill Association, various factories have to use foreign wheat because domestic wheat is insufficient. They have ordered nine ships from the American Wheat Affairs Office and one ship from Canada, Australia, the United States, etc., for a total of ten ships. All have been registered with the Social Affairs Bureau and have been dumped. Now that the Ministry of Finance is collecting foreign wheat tax in advance, each 100 catties, including additional tax, costs about 7 jiao in national currency, and each bag of flour costs about 3 jiao. At a time when grain prices are low, flour prices cannot be increased according to the tax rate, and the losses suffered cannot be compensated. Please telegram the department to exempt the foreign wheat ordered by various factories before the tax rules were announced from taxation in order to protect the factory capital. We hereby telegraph to you and ask for your approval. Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce.

City Land Bureau Announces Winter Grain Tax Collection Starting Today

The City Land Bureau yesterday issued a proclamation regarding the collection of the twenty-second year winter grain tax, stating in brief: The twenty-second year grain tax, reed tax, Jinshan assistance transport, garrison rent, etc., will be collected starting December 16th. For the Zhenru district, due to the autumn disaster of the twenty-first year, a reduction of 0.05 will be applied, resulting in an actual collection of 0.95. The remaining districts will continue to collect at the old rate. The assessment documents will detail this information. The deadline for payment is two months from the start of collection, expiring on February 15th of the twenty-third year. Those who fail to pay by the deadline will be subject to an additional 0.05 tax, with a continued deadline for two more months, expiring on April 15th. Failure to pay by this deadline will result in an additional 0.1 tax, as a penalty for delay.

Attending Representatives

Hong Xianting of Yide Company, Zhou Wende of Hengyu, Fang Yongyu of Xutongji, Zhuang Yisun of Meiyiji, Shen Weilin of Jiuxing, Gao Zairu of Guixing, Zhao Wenyu of Chengbao, Mu Wenkuan of Dongyu, Yu Shi'an of Longzhang, Yu Pengling of Taojinji, Kui Yanfang of Taili, Jin Hongtao of Tianren, Chen Binggang of Zhenyisanyi, Ye Qiyu of Yeguang, Dong Shusen of Qiu Cheng Qitang, Shen Huada of Fan Rulin, Cao Wenbao, Sun Shensheng of Qingji, Ji Xuan of Dalu, Li Songquan of Deli, Bao Yongquan of Gu Lanji, and over forty other people.

Chairman's Report

Chairman Kui Yanfang reported that the significance of today's meeting is profound. First, our industry must unite in the current environment. The water fee dispute is in its final five minutes. Since the beginning of April this year, the Public Works Bureau of the International Settlement decided to implement a tiered pricing system for the water company and also decided to establish a water fee committee to resolve all issues. Unexpectedly, the bureau's Director-General Zhong Si delayed implementation, resulting in the water fee dispute. Repeated suggestions from this association have been shelved, and the water company has intensified its oppression, such as cutting off the water to Bailifu and other areas, dismantling insufficient meters, and even cutting off public water taps that residents themselves installed, endangering the lives of over three thousand residents. This association and representatives from Deli Company went to the Public Works Bureau, but Director-General Zhong Si relied solely on the water company's side of the story, which is truly disheartening. This time, the joint struggle of Deli Company and residents is not just for themselves but for the common interests of our industry and residents within the settlement. According to the contract signed by the Public Works Bureau and the water company, there is absolutely no provision allowing the water company to cut off the water. The water company cannot cut off the water in houses where people live, which shows that the water company's actions are not allowed. The contract between the water company and users or owners stipulates that water can be cut off for non-payment, which conflicts with the basic contract and is naturally invalid. Users or owners consider the water fees agreed upon and have no reason not to pay. However, the water company is becoming increasingly bizarre, cutting off water for failure to pay surcharges, forcing the signing of meter installation contracts, and demanding payment of increased water fees without consent. It completely disregards the basic contract, does not file lawsuits in court according to the law, and endangers all residents, placing them in danger of life and property. Recently, due to the joint struggle of Deli Company and its tenants, our country's lawyers and courts have also paid attention to it. Deli Company and its tenants not only made the water company voluntarily offer discounts twice but also greatly contributed to our country's legal rights and those who enforce the law. This association is grateful to Deli Company and its tenants for their struggle for the public. If there are any actions that infringe on their legitimate rights and public interests, we will do our best to help. All our colleagues should act according to their conscience and rise up together so that Deli Company's goal of fighting for the dignity of tenants and reducing the burden on users can be achieved. I propose: (1) Send a letter to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, which will then forward it to the Shipping Association, stating that all water used by our country's ships should be purchased from our country's water company. (2) Send a letter to the municipal authorities, urging them to quickly have our country's water company handle the water supply for roads outside the settlement. (3) Send another letter to our organization, urging them to quickly drill artesian wells to achieve a lasting solution and reduce residents' living expenses.

Discussion Items

(1) The death of Jiang Yansheng, standing committee member and economic director of this association. Resolved: A representative will be sent to attend the memorial service. (2) Appointment of a new standing committee member. Resolved: Li Shuxiong will be appointed. (3) Appointment of a new director. Resolved: Shen Jixuan will be appointed. (4) Confidential. (5) According to a member's report, the water company is revising bills. Resolved: There is one revision, who knows if there will be a second, third, or endless revisions? Members should be notified that when they receive a revised bill, they should only pay after the water fee calculation is confirmed to be accurate and reasonable. (6) Notify members to declare to tenants within three months that starting from a certain month and day, tenants must handle their own water supply. The water fee included in the rent should be deducted by 7.5% of the rent, and the rent receipts should be revised. (7) Send a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, asking them to notify the Shipping Association that all water used by our country's ships should be purchased from our country's water company. Resolved: To be done. (8) Send a letter to the municipal government, urging our country's water company to quickly supply water to the area outside the settlement. Resolved: To be done.

Letter to the Public Works Bureau

The Real Estate Association requests the Public Works Bureau to stop the water company's high-pressure tactics of cutting off water. The original letter states: "We are writing to inform you that, according to a letter from our member, Deli Company (letter omitted from yesterday's newspaper), water is indispensable to human life and cannot be denied by anyone. In addition to drinking, it is also necessary for cleanliness. The cleaning slogans posted on trams show that the Public Works Bureau's Health Department also values this. Now, on the one hand, residents are encouraged to use tap water to clean and remove dirt early in the morning, before lunch, and before going to bed. On the other hand, the water company is allowed to cut off water, leaving residents without water to use, struggling to survive without food, drink, and in filth. This is both unreasonable and inhumane and is absolutely contradictory to the authorities' cleaning policies. Furthermore, if the water price is fixed, then the goods are genuine and the price is fair, and there is no room for compromise. Fair treatment can be said to exist. However, the water company previously charged 10% of the rent under the high-pressure tactic of cutting off water, and now it wants to use 15% as a basis, calculating three times the original rate for exceeding this. This proves that its water price is not fixed, and there is no difference between using more and using less. Its ultimate goal is simply to increase its unlimited profits by increasing 6% of the rent to 7.5%, then to 10%, and then to 15% or more. If the water company cuts off water to those who refuse to increase the price, then the large discounts should not be like the high water fee that breaks the principle of 'no increase in fees for meter installation.' The large discounts should be given. Cutting off water immediately, causing unlimited losses to owners and users, should be the responsibility of compensation. According to the information in the letter, we hereby request your bureau to inform the water company for investigation." This is addressed to the Director-General of the Shanghai Public Works Bureau of the International Settlement.

Letter to the Water Company

The association contributed its opinion on the meter installation and payment methods, and sent a letter to the water company, stating: "We are responding to your letter of November 17 regarding the method of installing separate water meters, etc. We hereby state that (1) the water fee after meter installation should be collected by the water company from the actual users; (2) each user should install a water meter, and the deposit or meter maintenance fee should be borne by the actual user; and (3) all water fees previously included in the rent should be deducted by the landlord to correct the actual amount of the rent. These are the association's long-standing objective views. Unfortunately, those involved at the time did not adopt the good examples of general water companies due to inaccurate observation and understanding, which caused many disputes and resulted in significant losses for non-actual users. Thinking about it now, it is simply a self-inflicted problem. In terms of law and fact, the water user is one party, the payer is another party, and controlling waste is best achieved by 'planning for oneself rather than planning for others' according to common human nature. In any case, it is like climbing a tree to catch fish. The association's views remain as above. In order to strive for practicality and benefit the public, we make the following technical contributions: (1) Installing water meters in iron boxes for water taps will definitely not cause any problems. There is absolutely no need to modify outdoor water pipes. (2) The water meter deposit can still be reduced and can be the same as that set in Nanshi and Zhabei. It is said that it used to be 18 yuan per unit, but now it is 24 yuan. (3) If the user is unwilling to pay the deposit, it is more convenient to pay a monthly meter maintenance fee of 2 jiao or a corresponding amount. (4) This type of separate meter is absolutely essential. It should immediately replace the impractical large meters and the originally sold adjustable-column separate meters. There should be no difficulty for the Water Division. As for the claim that the water company's capital burden will increase if the water meter deposit is not adopted, which will lead to an increase in water prices, it seems to be the case in theory. However, there are no deposits for equipment such as telephone and electric light meters. However, this is only for the sake of debate. The association only hopes that it will follow the existing methods of general water companies. However, it must be emphasized again that general water companies do not have water meter, deposit, or maintenance fees in addition to water and electricity meter deposits. Furthermore, this association believes that it is best to work together in a peaceful consultation, each holding their own views, to seek solutions to common difficulties. Therefore, it is not appropriate to cut off the water to put people in danger of life. On July 9, 1932, at the Lausanne Conference, British Prime Minister MacDonald said, 'Public prosperity depends on the prosperity of each individual,' which should be regarded as the golden rule. According to the above letter, we hereby reply, hoping that you will investigate and act accordingly." This is addressed to the British Shanghai Waterworks Company.

Land Owners in the Central District Submit Petition to the City Government to Expedite the Issuance of Practice Certificates

Jiang Hongbin, director of the Miscellaneous Grains and Cake Exchange, submitted a document to Mayor Wu yesterday to expedite the issuance of practice certificates for land in the central district. The document states, "We are submitting a petition for the prompt issuance of practice certificates for land in the central district, for which the land price has already been paid in full, so that we can conduct business. We obtained land in the 30th and 31st districts, totaling over 40 mu, during the first issuance of land in the central district of this city. It was originally scheduled to be paid in four installments, and each installment has been paid in full as scheduled, and receipts from the Land Bureau have been received. The final payment was made at the end of December last year, and it has been almost a year now. Although we have repeatedly applied for the issuance of these practice certificates, they have not yet been issued. Upon inquiry, we were told that it is impossible to issue two certificates for one piece of land because the original land practice certificate was not submitted by the original owner. We believe that the management of land certificates is to determine property rights, and it is true that two levies on one piece of land are not allowed. However, it is difficult to reconcile if we deliberately shelve the matter. Since the property rights of the original owner's land have disappeared due to the land being returned to the central district, the Land Bureau should be fully responsible for the return and cancellation of the original certificate. We paid the land price and obtained the land after fulfilling legal procedures, and the issuance of a certificate to clarify the property rights should not be delayed any further. If the original owner illegally refuses to submit the certificate and the matter is delayed indefinitely, it will not only damage the government's authority, but also make it difficult to demonstrate justice to future generations. Therefore, we hereby submit this petition and implore you to instruct the Land Bureau to issue the practice certificates for the land obtained in the central district as soon as possible, so that we can manage our properties and secure our property rights. We are grateful for your kindness." Sincerely submitted to Wu, Mayor of Shanghai Municipal Government.

Wang Fuhai Kidnapping Case: Police File Appeal, Affirming Chen Desheng and Others' Involvement, Requesting Court to Overturn Original Verdict

Wang Zilin from Funing, residing at No. 722 Weihaiwei Road, has been contracted by the Seven Departments to handle fertilizer and stones for many years. He has a successful career, owning assets worth hundreds of thousands. His wife, Yan, has only one daughter, who is married to Xu Yunsun, a native of Anhui working in the customs. For the sake of continuing his lineage, Wang took Zhang as a concubine, who gave birth to a son named Fuhai. He is four years old, clever and lively, and loved like a precious jewel. Unexpectedly, around 6 a.m. on April 27th of last year, while the child was sound asleep in the guest hall upstairs with his grandmother, kidnappers suddenly broke in through the back door. They went upstairs and took Fuhai from the blanket. Wang's mother was greatly alarmed and shouted. Zilin rushed down, disregarding his life, and tried to snatch Fuhai from the bandits. The accomplices of the bandits opened fire, injuring Wang's arm and causing him to fall to the ground. A stray bullet fatally wounded a maid named Li Tao. Fuhai was still abducted and hidden in a remote area of Chongming Island by the leader who hired a boat at the Huishan Wharf, demanding a huge ransom. Wang Zilin, already advanced in age, feared for his only biological son's life and paid a ransom of 40,000 yuan. Subsequently, the Hongkou police arrested two suspects, Wang Xiaosizi and Jiang Shihua, who were sentenced to imprisonment. However, the leader of the kidnapping gang was still at large, and there were no clues to be found. It wasn't until October 15th of this year that Wang Chengying, a Chinese detective of the Jiaru Road police station, and others arrested Chen Desheng, a native of Funing, Jiangbei. He confessed to committing a kidnapping case, namely the kidnapping of Wang Zilin's child Fuhai. He said that the leader was Yan Shirong, a relative of Wang. He confessed to the details of the kidnapping. The detectives apprehended Yan's wife, Chen, who confessed that it was Wang's accountant, Xiang Wenshan, who planned it. Xiang was then arrested and confessed the reason for the case: the instigator was Wang's wife, Yan, due to property disputes. She feared that after Fuhai grew up, the concubine Zhang would seize exclusive power. Therefore, she secretly conspired with her younger brother, Yan Shirong, and her son-in-law, Xu Yunsun, and others. Yan Shirong invited Jiangbei bandits Chen Desheng to carry out the kidnapping, and Wang's workers Yang Yuexiang and Chen Xiaosizi also helped as internal accomplices. The detectives also arrested Wang Yan, Xu Yunsun, Yang Lin, and others, and sent them to the First Special District Court along with Chen Desheng. Chen Desheng, Yan Wang, and Xiang Wenshan confessed without reservation, providing detailed testimonies. The others all denied involvement. During the second court hearing, they suddenly recanted, claiming to be completely unrelated. Although the plaintiff, Wang Zilin, was well aware of the underlying reasons, he did not pursue the matter due to certain relationships. As a result, all defendants were declared not guilty. The police lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, appealed against Chen Desheng, Yan Chen, and Xiang Wenshan, which the court approved. The others were released. Yesterday afternoon, Zhao Zheng, a judge from the Criminal Division of the Second High Court, along with Judges Jiang and Zhou, came to the criminal court to conduct a preliminary hearing. The police lawyer, Zhang, stated that the defendants had confessed in detail at the police station and during the original trial, vividly describing how they planned and carried out the kidnapping, which was consistent with the police's statements and without any contradictions. Furthermore, their attitude was firm, and Xiang Wenshan told the two workers, Yang and Chen, that they should not deny it, which was very intense. Therefore, he requested that the original judgment be overturned and that they be punished according to the law. When questioned, Chen Desheng, Yan Chen, and Xiang Wenshan denied their previous confessions, claiming that they were not made voluntarily and asking for understanding. The plaintiff, Wang Zilin, stated that the defendants were not present when Fuhai was kidnapped. Judge Zhao instructed that they be detained separately and that a date be set for the verdict.

A Lustful Man Encounters a "Honey Trap": A Rogue Cleverly Uses a Beauty Trap, Simple Country Folk Suffer Losses

Zhao Meisheng from Suzhou, nearly forty years old, is inherently lustful. His financial ability is not weak, and he is not stingy when it comes to buying pleasure. Therefore, he frequents brothels in Hanzhuang. However, his behavior is somewhat crude, making him easily manipulated. A man named Zhang, who knows Zhao well, set up a "honey trap" on the 14th of this month. After arranging everything carefully, he went to Zhao's residence upstairs at the Yonghe Pharmacy on Guizhou Road and invited Zhao out, saying that there was a beautiful girl named Liu Xiuying, who was young and beautiful. Although she came from a good family, she could be easily seduced. If Zhao was interested, he would not hesitate to introduce them. Zhao, who was easily swayed by hearsay and whose desires were piqued, did not consider the consequences and, after gathering his money, followed Zhang to find this paradise. On the way, they suddenly saw a young woman standing gracefully, seemingly waiting for someone. Zhang pointed to the woman and said to Zhao, "This is her." In reality, although the woman was young, her appearance was only average. However, Zhao, after being subjected to a few glances from the woman, was already captivated and considered her a celestial being. At that time, Zhang continued to act as a guide, and they went to the Qinghe Hotel on Zhejiang Road, opening a secret room to enjoy their intimate feelings. With Zhang's mission completed, he left. Zhao and the woman closed the door and were about to undress and get into bed when suddenly five strong men broke into the room. They were fierce. The leader, Liu Zhengyuan from Wuxi, claimed to be Xiuying's husband and accused Zhao of seducing a married woman. The other four, Liu Zhengting, Chen Huating, Zhang Yanlan, and Zhu Binshan, echoed his words and either slapped Zhao or kicked him. Zhao, outnumbered, could only plead. After beating him, Liu and the others took Zhao's long gown and the 22 yuan in his pocket. Because they still thought the amount was too small, they decided to force Zhao to negotiate somewhere else. As soon as they left the hotel, they were spotted by Cui Jinchuan, a detective from the Laozha police station. After inquiring about the situation, he brought them all back to the police station. After questioning by the head detective, Zhao and Liu Xiuying were released, and Liu Zhengyuan and the other four were detained. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Special District Court. Judge Qian Hongye conducted a preliminary hearing. The police lawyer, Zhang Shizhu, explained the circumstances of the case, stating that the defendants dared to use the "honey trap" to extort money, which was unforgivable. He requested that they be punished for the crime of intimidation and fraud. Then, Zhao Meisheng testified, saying that Zhang introduced him to Liu Xiuying and that he did not try to seduce her. However, Liu Xiuying sided with her husband, saying that Zhao and Zhang had been stalking her for days, leading her to be lured to the hotel. The defendant, Liu Zhengyuan, also testified that Xiuying was his wife and that yesterday, because she was lured to the hotel by Zhao and others, he and his friends went to catch them in the act. The others gave evasive answers. The court reviewed the testimonies and found that the defendants were clearly trying to cover up the truth. Immediately, the court declared the verdict: the defendants were found guilty of attempted extortion and each was fined 50 yuan. If they were unable to pay, they would be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. The defendants each posted 50 yuan bail. Those who could not post bail were remanded in custody pending execution of the sentence.

Gelling Agent Extracted from Yellow Okra Juice, a Raw Material for Liu Paper, Solidifies Itself 丨Invention by Dr. Xie Hui丨

The juice of yellow okra, produced in China, is a raw material for making machine-made "Lian Shi" and "Mao Bian" paper. It makes the paper smooth and prevents ink from bleeding when writing, making it widely used. The industrialist Tianxu Wosheng once encouraged farmers to plant it to increase by-products. However, okra juice has a disadvantage: it is not easy to store, and the market is sluggish, making it waste. Farmers suffer losses. Dr. Xie Hui, a chemistry professor at Jiaotong University, recognizing this problem, has been engaged in research. Now, he has been able to extract the gelling agent from the okra juice, making it solidify and can be stored for a long time. The experiment has been successful, and the industrial community has praised it highly. This is good news for improving China's agricultural products.

Lanzhou-Dihua Airmail Temporarily Suspended

According to the Shanghai Post Office, the Eurasia Aviation Corporation has announced that the Lanzhou-Dihua airmail service is suspended indefinitely. All airmail to Xinjiang via Lanzhou will be temporarily suspended.

Stamping Foreign Liquor: Chinese and Foreign Merchants Should Be Treated Equally, the Machine Industry Association Appeals to the Ministry of Finance for Review and Implementation

The Shanghai Machine-Made National Products Factory Association believes that the stamp tax on foreign liquor and alcohol is not applied consistently to Chinese and foreign merchants, causing hardship for domestic manufacturers. Yesterday, it appealed to the Ministry of Finance for equal treatment. The original appeal stated, "Regarding the tax on Chinese-made imitation foreign liquor and alcohol, please treat Chinese and foreign merchants equally." According to Article 1 of the Provisional Regulations on Foreign Liquor Tax issued by the Ministry of Finance in June of the 18th year of the Republic of China, "All foreign liquor sold within the country must pay taxes according to the provisions of these Regulations." Section 2 states, "The aforementioned foreign liquor, whether manufactured by foreigners or imitated by Chinese, or imported, is subject to these regulations." Currently, the Shanghai Baoshan Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Collection Sub-Bureau requires Chinese-made imitation foreign liquor to be stamped on each bottle. For imported goods, after tariff autonomy, the import tax rate on foreign liquor has been increased. Therefore, according to the principle of not taxing the same item twice, stamping is no longer required. However, most of the brandy foreign liquor consumed in the market

Foreigners Mostly Exploit Loopholes

The raw materials are imported in barrels, bottled and sold in China. According to the current import tax rate, barrelled foreign liquor is taxed at 50% of its value. Although it is unknown how the value is assessed, the tax rate for bottled liquor under the same item 378 is only one yuan and three jiao of customs gold per case of twelve quarts, which is about two jiao of national currency per bottle. However, according to the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Machine-Made Liquor Stamp Tax Rate Table set by the Jiangsu Stamp Tax Office, bottled brandy liquor is stamped at six jiao and five fen per bottle. Therefore, even if the tariff has been increased, it is still less than one-third of the original stamp tax rate. Imported goods from foreign merchants are exempt from stamping, while Chinese-made imitation foreign liquor is still subject to stamping. This is tantamount to protecting and promoting the sales of foreign liquor. Because foreign liquor is declared for import in barrels, paying 50% of the value, it is bottled with water, containing only half alcohol, which is equivalent to paying only 25% of the tax. Chinese merchants who purchase barrelled foreign liquor and bottle it with water for sale must not only pay 50% of the value for the import tax on raw materials but also pay a stamp tax of 30% of the value. If it contains half water, it is equivalent to paying 110% of the value. This is the first inequality between Chinese and foreign merchants in the collection of taxes on bottled liquor. Furthermore, according to Article 3 of the Provisional Regulations on Foreign Liquor Tax, the tax on spirits is 20 yuan per hundred jin. This was set in June of the 18th year of the Republic of China, which is the same as the 341st item in the Jiangsu Stamp Tax Office Special Stamp Tax Table, which stipulates that spirits and alcohol are taxed at 20 yuan per hundred jin and 1.5 yuan per English gallon. At that time, the import tariff was only 5% of the value, and the tax per gallon was only four fen of national currency. After tariff autonomy, it gradually increased. As of the amendment on May 22nd of this year, pure spirits are taxed at four jiao five fen six li of customs gold per gallon including surtax, which is about nine jiao one fen of national currency. Compared with the previous tariff, it has increased more than 22 times. Although the tax on poisonous denatured spirits has been reduced by about half, it is still about four jiao six fen of national currency, which is more than ten times higher than before. Foreign merchants' alcohol is used in factories located in the concessions. In addition to paying import taxes, there is no possibility of stamp duty. Chinese merchants' alcohol is used in factories located in Chinese territory. They must pay the same import tax, and they must also pay stamp duty. For example, the pharmaceutical industry uses it as an immersion agent, the hardware industry uses it to make varnish, and the cosmetics industry uses it in cologne. If the products are made by foreign merchants in factories located in the concessions, the alcohol used costs only nine jiao one fen per gallon. If the products are made by Chinese merchants in factories located in Chinese territory, then in addition to paying a tariff of nine jiao one fen per gallon, they must also pay a stamp tax of one yuan and five jiao. Regardless of its value, the tax burden is already disparate. For the same product, foreign merchants can sell it for nine jiao one fen, while Chinese merchants must sell it for two yuan four jiao one fen. Isn't this

Clearly Blocking the Road for Chinese Merchants

Turning it into a guarantee for foreign merchants, it is straight for a fish in an abyss, which will make Chinese circles, no rest of Bai factory place, the affairs of the world are not more unequal than this, the members and factories are the same without a way, I want a final solution is to come to the meeting to discuss, please immediately prepare a document from the club to submit to your department to solve it, the method is as follows, (1) the first clause of the Provisional Regulations on Foreign Liquor Tax, the second item of the original text, regardless of foreign manufacturers, Chinese imitations, and imports, it now belongs to the imported foreign liquor sold on the market, because the tariff has been increased, according to the principle of one thing not taxing twice, it can no longer be stamped, then all Chinese-imitated foreign liquor, purchased barrel bags of raw materials, and bottled, should be allowed to present the tax payment certificate that has been paid, with the same treatment, and no longer stamped, if there is no certificate that has been paid the same tax, it is manufactured and sold in China, then Chinese and foreign merchants should be stamped, so that the powers and responsibilities of the collection bureau are clear, and it will not exclude national goods for foreigners, (2) the tax rate in the third clause of the same chapter, the customs duty has been increased, and imports are slightly Customs duty, except for exemption from stamping, is originally aimed at those who manufacture and sell in China, because it has not been completed Customs duty, there is no certificate document collection, it should be taxed according to regulations, in order to prevent stealing and taking advantage of it, because according to the current import Ministry of Finance Approved: Flour Exported with Half Tax, Bran Exported as Usual

According to Heping News Agency, the Shanghai Flour Industry Association believes that more and more foreign flour is imported recently, and the sales of domestic flour have stagnated and the business has declined sharply. Special requests have been made to the Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi to cancel the export ban on wheat flour and approve tax-free exports in order to provide relief. After considering the situation, the Ministry of Finance has reviewed and approved the lifting of the ban on the export of wheat flour. It can be handled as is. As for wheat bran, which has never been banned from transportation, it is difficult to avoid taxes. The petition has been submitted to the Executive Yuan for notification. The flour industry's submission and the Ministry of Finance's approval are recorded as follows.

Flour Industry's Submission

Submit to the Department of Commerce for the export ban on rice and wheat, which has been canceled, and the flour is the same. I respectfully request the Department of Commerce to continue to lift the ban and export tax-free. The case of flour submitted for approval to continue to ban the export will expire on December 1 of this year. Now, in the flour market in our country, the production and sales have been greatly affected since the fall of the Northeast, coupled with the dumping of foreign flour and the bankruptcy of rural areas, the sales are increasingly sluggish. I am planning to submit a request to permanently lift the ban on export in order to find a way out. Recently, I read in the newspaper that the Executive Yuan's Yuanwu meeting has passed and canceled the export ban on rice and wheat. It has been issued to the provincial governments for implementation. I also read in your Department's order to the Jianghai Customs Superintendent, "In addition to instructing the Director-General of Customs to transfer orders to the customs directors of various countries, rice grains, wheat, sorghum, millet, buckwheat, corn, and other miscellaneous grains that were originally prohibited from transportation to foreign countries shall be prohibited from transportation and exempted from export tax. They are to be instructed to comply." Now the price of flour is falling, affecting the price of wheat. Commerce and rural areas are closely related. Now rice, wheat, and other miscellaneous grains have been uniformly lifted. For example, sesame seeds, which have always been subject to an export tax of five cents of silver per five hundred catties, are now approved for tax-free export. Flour is the same. Without the approval of tax-free export of Chinese flour, it is not enough to reject the influx of foreign flour. In addition, bran is wheat bran, an appendage of flour, and should be treated the same as No. 2, 3, and 4 flour. I respectfully request that your Department order the Jianghai Customs Superintendent and the Director-General of Customs to transfer orders to the customs directors of various customs to permanently lift the ban on export and exempt taxes in order to facilitate circulation and maintain the flour industry.

Approval of the Ministry of Finance

The Flour Industry Association received Order No. 179 from the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating that the case of the export ban on flour was originally handled by the Ministry of Finance upon order because of the food shortage caused by disasters in the country at that time. Now, the situation of oversupply and sluggish sales of agricultural products in various places is actually the opposite of what it was before. The request to lift the ban on the export of No. 2, 3, and 4 wheat flour can be approved. However, wheat flour has not been subject to customs duties. The current tax is still a special tax, which is obviously different from the customs duties on other grains. Therefore, it cannot be completely tax-free. It should still be taxed upon leaving the factory according to the regulations of the wheat flour special tax regulations. After the export, half of the actual tax amount will be refunded in order to comply with the regulations and encourage export. As for bran, most of it is for industrial use, with a large amount exported annually. It has never been banned from transportation and is inherently different from grains. It is difficult to be exempted from taxes in the same way. Moreover, this association submitted a request for tax exemption on wheat bran exports in July of this year, which was approved by this Ministry. It should be handled according to the case. In addition to forwarding the presentation and issuing orders separately, the approval is known. This approval.

First Batch: American Wheat Arrives Tomorrow Night, Unloading at Floating Buoy No. 16, Requesting Exemption from New Import Tax

The first batch of American wheat borrowed from the loan, shipped from Portland to Shanghai, was originally scheduled to arrive on Tuesday. Later, due to fog, the arrival date in Shanghai was delayed. Now, it has been confirmed that it will arrive tomorrow. However, since the arrival of the goods in Shanghai coincides with the announcement of increased tariffs on foreign rice and wheat, problems are bound to arise. The situation is urgently recorded as follows:

Unloading at Floating Buoy

The wheat in the ship totals 8,940 tons. Yesterday, the ship owner telegraphed that it had passed Japan and would arrive at the Wusongkou at 5 pm tomorrow. The pilots have been prepared here to take it into the Huangpu River tonight. However, because all the wheat on the ship has been sold, it will not dock at the Chinese warehouses, but will be anchored at Floating Buoys No. 16 and 17. The buyers will hire barges to unload the cargo alongside the ship. It is estimated that the hatch can be opened to unload the goods on Monday.

Tariff Issue

This batch of American wheat was originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 12th. Even if tariffs were levied, it could be imported before the new tax was implemented, and there would be no problem. Now, due to the fog, the ship is delayed. However, if it could follow the Pacific route, it could still arrive before the implementation of the tax. The delay is due to the ship owner taking a long detour around the ocean, causing the arrival date to be after the promulgation of the new tax. The error is not in the fog. After the ship arrives in Shanghai, the American Wheat Administration must negotiate with the ship owner about this matter.

Requesting Tax Exemption

If this batch of American wheat is paid according to the new tax, at least more than 40,000 yuan will be paid. Moreover, batches two, three, four, and five have been loaded and are about to arrive successively. If taxes are required, the tax rate for these five ships alone will be 200,000 yuan. Moreover, there are more large amounts of goods coming. The reporter learned yesterday that the American Wheat Administration has submitted this matter to the central government, stating that a large part of the American wheat shipped to Shanghai on loan will be used for disaster relief (the Yellow River disaster will also use American wheat as a substitute for relief). The central government should be requested to exempt the import tax. The submission has been made and may be approved for tax exemption.

Father of Kim Seok: Urges the Authorities Again to Negotiate and Submits a Letter to the French Central Police Station Requesting Release

Since Kim Seok, a naturalized Korean, was arrested, various sectors have spoken out in support, but he has not yet been released. His father, Kim Young-tak (i.e., Kim Cheol), yesterday submitted separate letters to the Municipal Government and the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, requesting speedy negotiations. The original submissions are recorded separately as follows:

Submitting to the Municipal Government

Regarding a submission: I, the submitter Zi Jinzhe, was illegally arrested in the French Concession by the French Central Police Station, with the assistance of the Japanese Consulate General. I, the submitter, petitioned your office to protest to the Japanese Consul General, but the Japanese Consulate General has been unreasonable and has not released me. In addition to requesting another protest to the Japanese Consul General, I request a serious protest to the French Consul General. Zi Jinzhe, along with the submitter, was naturalized as a Chinese citizen in the eighteenth year of the Republic (copy attached), and has resided at 446 Avenue Petain in the French Concession for several years. The French Concession is Chinese territory, and Zi Jinzhe is a citizen of the Republic of China. Even if there is suspicion of a crime, it should be under the jurisdiction of the Chinese court. No country other than China can arrest, deliver to a non-Chinese court, detain, or judge him. Now, the French Central Police Station, acting on the instructions of the Japanese Consulate General, has assisted in the illegal arrest of a Chinese citizen residing within its concession and, after detaining him at the police station, handed him over to the Japanese Consulate General's staff for detention. This is an infringement of our national sovereignty. Although the submitter's representatives, Li Shichang and lawyer Xu Jie, brought the submitter's and Zi Jinzhe's nationality permits to inquire, the French Central Police Station claimed that it did not know that Zi Jinzhe had been naturalized as a Chinese citizen and made the excuse that Zi Jinzhe claimed to be of Korean nationality. The reason why the submitter and his son naturalized as Chinese citizens was to enjoy the rights granted to Chinese citizens by the Chinese state and to fulfill the obligations of Chinese citizens to the Chinese state. Zi Jinzhe is not naive or ignorant, so how could he voluntarily abandon the rights granted to him by the Chinese state and willingly claim to be of Korean nationality? When the submitter's representative, lawyer Xu Jie, asked the police station if there was a record of his confession that he claimed to be of Korean nationality, they said no. Therefore, the French Central Police Station's claim that Zi Jinzhe claimed to be of Korean nationality is entirely a fabrication. Furthermore, the submitter and his son Zhezhe were illegally arrested by the Japanese Consulate General in the French Concession in November of last year. After your office and various French organizations protested strongly and presented the submitter's and Zhezhe's naturalization permits, they were sent back to the French Police Station for release. The matter involved several countries, and the French Police Station was the most important party involved. Therefore, the French Police Station already knew that Zi Jinzhe was a Chinese citizen. The reason why they claimed not to know was to shirk the responsibility of delivering him. This is very obvious. Even if they did not know that Zi Jinzhe had been naturalized as a Chinese citizen at the time and mistakenly delivered him, now that the submitter's representative has presented the naturalization certificate to prove it, the French Police Station is obliged to demand that the Japanese Consulate General return Zi Jinzhe. After repeated negotiations, the French Central Police Station turned a deaf ear. Their contempt for our national authority has reached its extreme. Moreover, Zi Jinzhe is not the only naturalized Chinese citizen residing in the French Concession. If this precedent is set, who will not be in danger? The naturalization clause of the Nationality Law is equivalent to a dead letter, and the naturalized citizens will lose all respect for the country. Moreover, it is recently learned that Zi Jinzhe is about to be sent to Japan. In order to request your office to protest to the Japanese Consulate General again, please issue a swift protest to the French Consul General. I would be most grateful. I respectfully submit this to Wu, Mayor of the Shanghai Municipal Government.

Submitting to the Foreign Affairs Office

Regarding a submission: My eldest son, Zi Jinzhe, formerly of Korean nationality, acquired Chinese nationality on October 5th of the eighteenth year of the Republic, along with the submitter, and holds Nationality Permit No. 67 of the Ministry of the Interior (film attached). He established residence in the French Concession of Shanghai. On November 22nd of this year, he was illegally arrested at 451 Route Pere Robert in the French Concession by the French Central Police Station with the assistance of the Japanese Consulate General. After arriving at the French Central Police Station, he was immediately handed over to the Japanese Consulate General. The submitter's representatives, lawyers Li Shichang and Xu Jie, presented the submitter's and Zi Jinzhe's nationality permits and negotiated with the French Central Police Station. The French Central Police Station claimed that they did not know that Zi Jinzhe had been naturalized as a Chinese citizen at the time. Furthermore, lawyers Xu Jie and Lou Yunmei, on behalf of the submitter, requested the French Consul General to notify the Japanese Consul General to release Zi Jinzhe, and submitted it to the Shanghai Municipal Government to protest to the Japanese Consulate General. Zi Jinzhe is a Chinese citizen and the French Concession is Chinese territory. The illegal arrest by the Japanese Consulate General is an infringement of national sovereignty. The French Central Police Station's assistance in the arrest and delivery not only violates the agreement regarding the establishment of a Chinese court in the French Concession of Shanghai, but also shows contempt for our entire country. Although there have been negotiations and protests, the Japanese Consul General has delayed his release. It is recently learned that Zi Jinzhe is about to be sent to Japan. The matter concerns individual legal interests, which are small, but concerns national authority, which is great. Therefore, I especially submit this to your office. In addition to protesting to the Japanese and French Consulates General separately, please forward this to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for serious negotiations so that Zi Jinzhe can be released as soon as possible and Chinese sovereignty can be protected. I would be most grateful. I respectfully submit this to Yu, Director of the Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the National Government in Shanghai.

Method of Notifying for Partial Pickup of Goods Storage Fees in Batches on Two Railways

A circular from the Traffic Department of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways stated: After full carloads of goods arrive, if they are picked up in batches (for example, if 10 tons have been picked up from a 25-ton load, leaving 15 tons), the remaining goods exceed the prescribed free storage period.

Post Office Issues Commemorative Stamps with Portrait of Chen Qimei - Two Denominations: One Cent and Fifty Cents

The Shanghai Post Office has recently issued two new commemorative stamps with the portrait of a martyr, in the denominations of one cent and fifty cents. Both feature the portrait of Chen Qimei. According to the post office, the following types have also been issued successively before: two types of stamps with the portrait of Deng Keng, half cent and two and a half cents; two types of stamps with the portrait of Liao Zhongkai, three cents and thirty cents; two types of stamps with the portrait of Zhu Zhixin, eight cents and thirteen cents; two types of stamps with the portrait of Song Jiaoren, ten cents and seventeen cents; and two types of stamps with the portrait of Huang Xing, twenty cents and forty cents. Adding the two newly issued stamps, the whole set has portraits of six martyrs.

After the time has passed, should the storage fee be calculated according to the whole car or another price rate? As there are no explicit regulations, it is difficult to follow. This has been discussed and resolved at the Fourth Traffic Conference. The storage fee should be calculated separately on the cargo ticket and loose cargo should be charged according to the proportion of the freight. This will be recorded. The price rate for this storage fee should be based on the freight paid at the time of loading. Although the actual storage of goods picked up in batches from a full carload is less than a full car, the freight paid at the time of loading is calculated based on the full car. The storage fee should be collected according to the weight of the remaining part (less than one ton is counted as one ton) and calculated as the storage fee for the full car. As for loose cargo, it should be charged according to the proportion of the freight weight. This circular is issued urgently and should be followed.

Yang Bingxun's Handling of the Reproduction of Shorthand Studies - Victims Can Enroll for Free

Regarding the dispute of counterfeiting and reprinting Bingxun's shorthand studies, which was published in the newspapers a few days ago, the inventor Yang Bingxun has found out that it was indeed done by the Nanjing YMCA. The association hired Zhang Mianzhi to privately set up a Chinese shorthand course, reprinted Bingxun's shorthand textbook, irrationally attempted to modify Bingxun's shorthand symbols, making it difficult for students to learn, and used the name of guaranteeing job introductions to seduce young people. In order to maintain the reputation of Bingxun's shorthand and protect the studies of young people, victims can use the tuition receipts issued by the YMCA and the reprinted textbooks or mimeographed handouts to register at the Bingxun Shorthand School in Gaoshou Lane, Haining Road, Shanghai, by registered mail. Mr. Yang will be responsible for teaching, whether in person or by correspondence, and will not charge additional tuition. It is heard that similar counterfeit incidents have also occurred in Hangzhou and other places. Victims will also receive the same treatment.

Shanghai Hospital's New President System

The board of directors of the Shanghai Hospital in Nanshi, which has long had a dual-leader system of Director of Medical Affairs and Director of Administrative Affairs, decided to amend the hospital's articles of association this winter due to the hospital's poor performance, and switch to a president system. They also drafted a reorganization plan, intending to seek out competent talent to serve as president. Yesterday, the hospital's board of directors held a meeting, with directors Huang Hanzhi, Hong Kui, Gu Xinyi, Qin Yanqi, Shen Gao, Zhang Binghui, Yao Xinzhi, Huang Yunchen, and other eight people present. After discussion, they were not very satisfied with the current Director of Medical Affairs, Zhou Chuliang. However, as there were no suitable candidates for the time being, it was decided that Director of Medical Affairs Zhou would temporarily act as the president for a term of three months, receiving his original salary. Director Shen Gao was also asked to supervise and improve the hospital according to the reorganization plan, and report to the board of directors for review after the term expired. The meeting adjourned.

Organization Minister of the Communist Seamen's Union, Li Aide, Arrested

Guangdong native, Zeng Bao, also known as Li Aide, is the current organization minister of the Communist Seamen's Union (referred to as the Seamen's Union). He formerly served as the secretary and standing committee member of the union. He was arrested the day before yesterday by the Public Security Bureau and the police in Tangshan Road, Jingzhou Road, and sent to the No. 2 Branch of the High Court. The police lawyer Li Zhishan said that the defendant confessed to arriving in Shanghai on the 12th on the Taikoo liner "Guangdong" from Guangdong. After investigation by the police, the liner could not arrive in Shanghai until the 14th, which shows that his statements were false. Because the police still needed to investigate, a request was made to postpone the hearing. Subsequently, the Public Security Bureau obtained a certificate from the offender Yuan Ziqing, proving that he was a colleague when he served on the Standing Committee of the Seamen's Union. Judge Zhou questioned Zeng once and ordered him to be remanded in custody and re-examined at a later date. A certain evening newspaper reported that Zeng was a lieutenant of the Communist Navy. This is actually a mistake for the Standing Committee of the Seamen's Union, because the Communist Party has never been heard to have a naval organization.

Feng Wenfeng's Calligraphy is Famous in Shanghai

The female calligrapher Feng Wenfeng is the daughter of Feng Shihhan, a epigraphist from Heshan. Shihhan had a rich collection of steles and wrote official script for more than thirty years. Miss Feng personally received his instruction, and is proficient in seal, official, regular, and cursive scripts. Ten years ago, she founded a women's calligraphy and painting school in Hong Kong. More than 100 graduates have made a name for themselves in the art world. Many people in South China who love calligraphy and painting have Miss Feng's works. Recently, Ye Gongchuo, Wang Yiting, Huang Binlang, Pan Lanshi, Wu Tiecheng, Lu Danlin, and others have helped her to set calligraphy rates. Those who seek her calligraphy are very enthusiastic. The Wenyi Company on Sijing Road collects the requests. Letters requesting price examples can be mailed to Deng's residence at 1760 Haining Road.

Qin Shengjie's Painting Exhibition Opens at the Ningbo Fellow Association

The landscape painting exhibition by the famous Liangxi painter Qin Shengjie and the exhibition of ancient calligraphy and paintings in his family collection opened yesterday on the fourth floor of the Ningbo Fellow Association on Xizang Road. The exhibition will last for four days and will end next Monday. Although it was raining yesterday, no less than four or five hundred people visited from morning to dusk. In the previous Qing dynasty, the two Qins were the most famous painters in Wuxi, and Shengjie is the great-grandson of Mr. Yiting. For generations, his family has been engaged in painting, and his family's knowledge is profound. He used to serve in the Ministry of Communications in the former capital. In his spare time, he immersed himself in the art world, and his attainments became more and more refined. Elder Fanshan once praised his works as being close to Yushan in elegance, and his style can be seen. He lamented the decline of Chinese painting, and specially exhibited his most refined works, as well as dozens of ancient calligraphy and paintings by famous artists of the Song, Yuan, Ming, and Qing dynasties in his family collection for appreciation. These ancient calligraphy and paintings are not only exquisite in their selection, but also, because they are from the collection of generations of painters, most of them are the masterpieces of various famous artists, and they are even more valuable for study. Therefore, the news spread widely and viewers followed closely. In addition to his own works, Mr. Qin is also willing to part with some of the ancient calligraphy and paintings for enthusiasts. It is heard that more than 20 pieces have been acquired by those who were quick to act.

The Establishment of the Xiehe Amateur Opera Troupe

Famous amateur opera singers He Jingshan, Xie Wenyuan, Xu Chengxu, Guo Xiaoxiao, Zhao Peixin, Sun Lanting, Gong Zhaoxiong, Dai Ronggui, etc., seeing that Peking opera will follow in the footsteps of Kun opera and be increasingly damaged, in order to preserve the national essence, organized the Xiehe Amateur Opera Troupe, specializing in the study of drama theory and rhyme. The association is located at the intersection of Xizang Road and Route Doumer. Yesterday, it was officially announced that the troupe has been established. Celebrities such as Du Yuesheng, Huang Jinrong, Zhang Xiaolin, Wang Xiaolai, Yu Qiaqing, Yuan Ludeng, and famous actors such as Mei Lanfang and Cheng Yanqiu have all given calligraphy scrolls and paintings as gifts. It is heard that the members of the association are limited to those who already have a foundation in drama theory, with a quota of 30 people. The membership fee is ten yuan, and the monthly membership fee is five yuan. The quota has already been met. They are currently looking for experienced opera singers to be instructors.
