Improvement of Telegraph Business in the Past Year (Part 2)

— Liu Junxiang

(8) Entrust China Travel Service to collect travel telegrams Travelers who want to inform their relatives and friends of their whereabouts at the port or station, but the telegraph bureau may not be nearby, so they have no way to achieve their purpose. Even if the telegraph bureau is nearby, the berthing of the boat and vehicle is only temporary, all the time

Important Information for Telegram Inquiries

— Qinghua

(II) Sages for Telegram Inquiries:

1. Correcting or Supplementing the Recipient's Name and Address: If, after sending a telegram, the sender discovers that the recipient's name and address were written incorrectly, or if they receive a notification from the telegraph office that the telegram cannot be delivered due to an unclear or incorrect recipient name and address, they may present the original telegram receipt to the telegraph office and send a paid official telegram to correct or supplement the recipient's name and address. For example, if the original telegram was "Huafeng Company, Beijing Road, Shanghai," and it cannot be delivered due to an unclear address, the sender may request a supplement to "Huafeng Company, Donghai Lane, Beijing Road." Or, if the original telegram was "Mr. So-and-so, Central Trading Company, Nanjing," and after sending the telegram, the sender suddenly receives a telegram or letter from the recipient stating that they have moved to the Overseas Chinese Hotel, they may request a correction to "Mr. So-and-so, Overseas Chinese Hotel, Nanjing," so that the receiving office can attempt delivery again.

2. Correcting or Supplementing the Text: If, after sending a telegram, the sender discovers an error in the text, they may present the original telegram receipt to the telegraph office and send a paid official telegram to correct the text. For example, if the original telegram text was "Funds can be remitted on the 6th," and due to a miscalculation of the date, it is intended to change it to the 7th, a request can be made to change the second character "six" to "seven." Additionally, if the recipient has doubts about a certain sentence in the received telegram and sends a paid official telegram to inquire, the sending office, upon receiving this official telegram, will notify the sender. If the sender wants to clarify things for the recipient, they can supplement the text. For example, if the original telegram text contains the phrase "Goods not shipped," and the recipient is in urgent need of the goods and does not understand why the sender has not shipped them, or suspects that the character "not" is a mistake for "already," and sends a paid official telegram to inquire, the sender may supplement the original telegram text to "Goods damaged, delayed shipment." In the above situation, the paid official telegram fee for the recipient's request to resend the three characters "Goods not shipped" cannot be refunded. The paid official telegram fee for the sender's supplemental text should also be paid separately, because the telegraph office is not at fault.

3. Canceling a Telegram: If, after sending a telegram, the sender wishes to cancel it for some reason, they may present the original telegram receipt to the telegraph office and send a paid official telegram to cancel the original telegram. This paid official telegram is charged at a rate of only four characters. If the original telegram has already been delivered to the recipient, the receiving office will notify the recipient to cancel the original telegram, rendering it invalid.

4. Inquiring About No Reply: If, after sending a telegram, the sender waits a long time and the recipient still has not replied, they may send a paid official telegram to inquire. There are two ways to inquire: (1) Inquire whether the telegram has been delivered properly. (2) Inquire why the recipient has not sent a reply telegram. Both of these paid official telegrams require prepayment of the reply telegram fee. If a reply from the receiving office by mail is desired, only the postage for the reply letter needs to be prepaid.

5. Inquiring About the Recipient's Registered Abbreviation: To save on telegram fees, if the recipient has a registered abbreviation at the receiving office, the sender can use the registered abbreviation instead of the recipient's name and address. However, if the memory is unclear, the telegraph office can be consulted for the telegram registration compilation. However, if there are errors in the registered abbreviations published in the compilation, or if the recipient has already terminated the registration, the telegraph office is not responsible if the telegram cannot be delivered.

6. Inquiring About Telegram Rates: If the sender needs to inquire about domestic or international telegram rates, they can use the telephone or visit the telegraph office in person to inquire. If many telegrams are sent each month, a rate table can be obtained from the telegraph office for reference at any time.

7. Inquiring About Line Conditions: To facilitate the sender in specifying the line through which the telegram is transmitted, the line conditions can be inquired about by telephone or in person at the telegraph office at any time. However, the telegraph office delivers received telegrams according to regulations, using the fastest transmission line. Only the transmission lines for international telegrams are divided into wireless and submarine cable. The sender can specify any of them arbitrarily. In general, wireless circuits are mostly direct circuits and use high-speed automatic telegraphy transmission (not manual telegraphy), so they are extremely fast and accurate.

8. Applying for a Refund: The refund of telegram fees should be applied for by the payer (i.e., the sender) to the sending office within six months from the date of sending the telegram. (However, the refund of prepaid reply fees should be applied for within three months.) If a refund is requested due to excessive delays or non-delivery of the telegram, a certificate issued by the receiving office or the recipient should be attached (in case of delayed telegrams, the original copy of the telegram received by the recipient can also be attached). If a refund is requested due to errors in the telegram, the original copy of the telegram received by the recipient should be attached. However, it should be noted that if the recipient has already inquired about and corrected the telegram error with the receiving office, or has inquired about and corrected it with the sending office using a paid official telegram, a refund cannot be applied for again.

Sending telegrams is also particularly difficult. In view of this, the Ministry of Communications, for the convenience of travelers, has specially launched a type of travel telegram, entrusting the China Travel Service, which has been handling travel business for many years, to conduct pilot projects in Nanjing, Shanghai, Peiping, Tianjin, Hankou, and Qingdao. The results were good and immediately considered for promotion. When travelers travel to the above-mentioned places, when boats and vehicles are parked, if they want to send ordinary urgent domestic telegrams, they can hand them over to the China Travel Service or the reception staff dispatched by the company for collection and forwarding. In addition to the long price, no handling fee will be charged. This is the convenience of communication without extra cost.

9. Creating Social Telegrams: In daily social interactions, the people of our country almost exclusively correspond through Western letters, and rarely send telegrams. This is because the people of our country have not yet developed the habit of using telegrams, and the high cost of telegrams is also a major reason. The Ministry of Communications originally had a New Year's telegram, which was open once every year around New Year's and Christmas, charging a quarter of the ordinary telegram price. However, the time limit for this telegram was limited, and the scope was too small, so the effect was not significant. Now it has been expanded into social telegrams, which can be used for celebrations of New Year, Christmas, weddings, birthdays, childbirth, opening, and promotion, condolences for funerals and illnesses, and thanks for the above-mentioned matters. The price per word is two cents for Chinese within the province, four cents for between provinces, and double for English. Moreover, for this telegram, not only can the receiving office provide free translation of incoming telegrams, but the sending office can also provide free translation of outgoing telegrams. The procedure is simple, the transmission is fast, and the cost is low. Its benefits to social interaction are truly significant, and for the telegraph business itself, it is no less than opening up a new field. Its future development can be predicted.

10. Newly Compiled Roman Alphabet Telegraph Code: The telegraph code numbers used in our country use four numbers to replace one Chinese character. Now, the Ministry of Communications has recompiled a new edition of the clear and secret code, improving the content. The most distinctive feature is that each Chinese character is not only affixed with a numeric code as before, but also a Roman alphabet code. The Roman alphabet code is composed of three Roman letters, and each group replaces one Chinese character. The sender arranges the groups of Roman letters in sequence, and then divides them into foreign words of ten letters each. In this way, ten Chinese characters can be replaced by three foreign language cipher words consisting of thirty Roman letters. The current international rates are extremely expensive, requiring two or three yuan per word. If this method is used, a lot of money can be saved, which is particularly convenient for overseas Chinese to communicate with their motherland.

In summary, the improvements in telegraph business within a year have been significant. From the perspective of the business itself, backlogs have been eliminated, and the business has been expanded. From the perspective of senders and receivers, costs have been reduced, telegrams are sent more conveniently, and telegrams are received more quickly. In short, the promoters strive to achieve maximum results with maximum effort, and senders and receivers can enjoy the highest communication convenience with the lowest cost. If we can continue to move forward in this direction, the future of the telegraph business is promising.

New Discovery of Positive Light Electrons

— Zhang

As far as we know, atoms are only two basic electrical units, that is: negative light electrons (ElectronNegatif) and positive heavy electrons (ProntonPassitif). However, British scholar Blackett and Italian young scholar Occhialina photographed the movement of the above two types of electrons and discovered a third particle whose weight is lighter than that of positive heavy electrons. As a result, the basic electrical unit positive light electron, which is recently recognized by the scientific community, was established.

The new electron differs from other electrons in two ways: first, it carries a positive charge; second, its life lasts only a few thousandths of a second. The new electrical unit has already been photographed by the Cambridge Laboratory in the UK and can be identified on the photos.

The above-mentioned British and Italian scholars also proved that although the new electron and the positron that make up the atom carry the same type of electricity, its weight is 1,800 times lighter than that of the electron, and when it encounters a negative electron, the life of the positive electron immediately stops. Its only expression of survival is a sudden emission of radiation during its tremor. There are now more than twenty photographs showing several light tubes of new electrons, and their latent power is as high as hundreds of millions of volts.

Telegram System Between Japan and "Manchukuo" (Part 1)

— Translated by Ye Zhonghua

This article was published in the September issue of Japan's "Teishin Zasshi" and was written by a Japanese national from the Foreign Correspondence Section of the Ministry of Communications' Telegraph Bureau. Its purpose is to explain the current situation of Japan's control over the Eastern Province's telecommunications administration. The article involves a review of Japan's management of the Eastern Province's telecommunications administration before the September 18th Incident, which can provide a glimpse into the historical stages of Japan's aggression against our country's telecommunications administration. Therefore, it is urgently translated to share with the people of our country. (Translator's note)

On August 31, the Ministry of Communications issued Instructions No. 35 and No. 36, formulating the Japan-"Manchukuo" Telegram Regulations and the Japan-"Manchukuo" Wireless Telegram Regulations, which were implemented on September 1. At the same time, the original Sino-Japanese Telegram Regulations and Sino-Japanese Wireless Telegram Regulations were declared abolished. These new regulations are closely related to the telecommunications and telephone services of the Eastern Province, both Manchurias, the Daodjie territory, and "Manchukuo," which are unified and operated by the Manchuria Telecommunications and Telephone Corporation, which goes without saying. Its main purpose is that the telegram system between the Kwantung Leased Territory and the South Manchuria Railway Affiliated Area and Japan, and the telegram system between "Manchukuo" and Japan have different prices and other handling methods. These two jurisdictions are very inconvenient due to geographical relationships. This unified plan is to equalize the prices and handle them in the same way in both jurisdictions. Before explaining the revised telegram system between Japan and "Manchukuo," we should first briefly describe the telecommunications business that Japan used to operate in Manchuria.

Japan's Telecommunications Business in Manchuria

To understand Japan's telecommunications and telephone business in Manchuria, we must at least go back to the era of the Russo-Japanese War in the 37th and 38th years of the Meiji era. At that time, Japan had set up military telecommunications and telephone lines in various parts of Manchuria during the war. When the war ended, Japan leased the Kwantung Leased Territory and the South Manchuria Railway Affiliated Area according to the Treaty of Portsmouth. At the same time, the submarine cables laid between Lushun and Zhifu and the cables in the South Manchuria Railway Affiliated Area were also included. The handling and use of the above cables and submarine cables were based on the treaty signed by the Chinese and Japanese governments in the 41st year of the Meiji era, and the communication of telecommunications between the Kwantung Leased Territory and the South Manchuria Railway Affiliated Area and China ("Manchukuo") was also implemented according to the above treaty. At the time of the Manchurian Incident, all telecommunications connections between the Kwantung Leased Territory and the South Manchuria Railway Affiliated Area and today's "Manchukuo" were only in Changchun, Tieling, Shenyang Yuanyang, Niuzhuang, and Andong. Its main methods of use were (1) Sino-Japanese cables, which were connected at the boundary of the South Manchuria Railway Affiliated Area, for the use of telegrams between the Kwantung Leased Territory and the South Manchuria Railway Affiliated Area and China (including Manchuria) and other countries outside China. Communication to the Japanese mainland had not yet been opened. (2) That is, Japanese telecommunications receiving and sending offices were set up in the above six Chinese telecommunications bureaus to connect with the Japanese bureaus in the affiliated area. This telecommunications connection was for Japan's exclusive use and was handled in the same way as the domestic communication (referring to the Japanese mainland) of the Japanese bureaus in the affiliated area. After the Manchurian Incident, telecommunications connection lines inside and outside the affiliated area were added, and direct communication between the North Manchuria area and the Japanese mainland was also opened. This point will be further elaborated on below.

The above-mentioned telecommunications connection between Japan and "Manchukuo" was only along the South Manchuria Railway Affiliated Area. Up to today, the communication facilities between Japan and "Manchukuo" have been completely changed after the Manchuria Telecommunications and Telephone Corporation invested in the operation, and the company operates as a whole!

Telecommunications Business between the Kwantung Leased Territory and the South Manchuria Railway Affiliated Area and Japan

The telecommunications business in the Kwantung Leased Territory and the South Manchuria Railway Affiliated Area is different from other Japanese colonies because it is special. Therefore, the telecommunications system between the area and Japan is also different from domestic telegrams or colonial telegrams in Japan. However, the difference lies in the regulations on prices, which should follow the old Sino-Japanese telegram system. As for other items, they are all handled in the same way as domestic telegrams in Japan. (The price of Sino-Japanese telegrams is omitted)

Telecommunications Business between "Manchukuo" and Japan

The connection lines in the six locations of the South Manchuria Railway Affiliated Area were exclusively for communication between the Kwantung Leased Territory and the Affiliated Area and China and other countries outside China. Domestic communication in Japan could not be used as an example. Therefore, there was no direct telecommunications connection between Japan and the current "Manchukuo" before the Manchurian Incident. Therefore, in the past, communication between "Manchukuo" and Japan had to be transferred through the submarine cables between Nagasaki and Shanghai, or between Qingdao and Sasebo, and according to the expensive prices of Chinese landlines. On the one hand, Sino-Japanese telegrams only reached the post offices along the South Manchuria Railway Affiliated Area. In addition, there was no other proper communication method, so the inconvenience of communication for Japanese residents in Manchuria until recently was beyond imagination.

South Manchuria News Agency: Domestic Chinese Telegram Price Reduction

The name and address of the recipient of a Chinese telegram often exceed ten characters due to the nature of Chinese characters. Therefore, each telegram fee often costs one or two yuan, so people are reluctant to use telegrams. The Ministry of Communications is now reducing prices from January 1 next year for the purpose of thoroughly facilitating public communication and developing business, as follows:

(1) The name and address of the recipient of a domestic Chinese telegram and the name of the receiving place do not exceed 15 characters, all are charged as five characters, and if this is exceeded, the fee is added by the character.

(2) For those who use telephone numbers instead of addresses, the name of the recipient and the name of the receiving place are charged as four characters in total.

(3) Those who use telegram registration instead of name and address will still be charged according to the regulations, that is, including the name of the receiving place, Chinese Mingyu telegrams will be charged as three characters, and Chinese password telegrams will be charged as two characters.

(4) For split telegrams, add three characters for each additional recipient's name and address. After the above method is implemented, an ordinary 20-character telegram (assuming the name and address is 15 characters and the telegram text is 5 characters) will only be charged as ten characters, which is equivalent to a 50% discount, just like a big price reduction in a store!

Reduction in the Price of Domestic Urgent Telegrams

Domestic urgent telegrams are charged three times the price of ordinary telegrams. The Ministry of Communications is now reducing the fee to twice the price of ordinary telegrams from January 1 next year to facilitate merchants and bring it in line with international urgent telegram fees. After this method is implemented, merchants who send urgent telegrams for urgent business information can save one-third of the cost.

Plan to Improve Telegram Receiving and Sending Procedures

The Ministry of Communications recently convened personnel in charge of receiving and sending telegrams from the telegraph bureaus and radio stations in Beijing and Shanghai to the ministry to hold a meeting to study the improvement of telegram receiving and sending procedures in order to increase the speed of telegram transmission. It is reported that the results were very satisfactory. The principle decided was to reduce all unnecessary procedures and strive to send telegrams as soon as they are received, and reduce delays at the receiving and sending offices. Procedures such as registration flow and calculation of the fees for ledger telegrams (that is, telegrams sent by business firms that have prepaid telegram fees and do not pay for telegrams by the telegram) are handled after the telegrams are sent. In this way, telegrams can be sent quickly on the one hand, and senders do not have to wait for a long time and waste time on the other hand, which is a major improvement in telegram business.

Classical and Modern

— Zilin

Yes, everything here is modern. The lights, beds, windows, sofas, dressing tables, and the color of the walls, although not as exaggerated as the "subjective" decoration advertised, but at least it cannot be regarded as modern. Even the waiters are very young, with their hair combed smoothly and wearing neat, modern uniforms.

When I walked into that newly opened hotel, I first felt that Shanghai was really different from before and had become much more modern. At the same time, I also thought of our traditional Chinese decorative art that emphasizes symmetry and balance, such as the couplets hanging in my home before, "A window contains the eternal snow of the Western Ridge, and boats moor at the Eastern Ying from ten thousand miles away." Now it has been broken through by modernity.

But when I opened the window, I immediately smelled a puff of opium smoke coming from the window next door. At this time, I was fully aware that I had returned to China. Then, from the window on the left, came the sound of mahjong tiles clashing and women laughing.

But strangely, in such a modernly equipped place, there are very few modern young men to be seen. Most of those who come and go are black men wearing melon-shaped hats and dark crystal glasses. They are a bit like the heads of some agencies, or small and medium-sized merchants and landlords who have come to Shanghai from the mainland recently. Later, I read a book by Mu Shiying called "Cemetery," and then I suddenly realized that the modern young people were probably dancing jazz with more modern girls in more modern places than here. I didn't expect that after not coming to Shanghai for a few years, even I have become an outdated person!

The night is getting deeper, but there are still many women coming and going in the corridor. Long eyebrows, flat noses, long earrings, black hair hanging in front of their foreheads, collars so high that they can't turn their necks, blood-red lips, two-inch high-heeled shoes. I really haven't seen Chinese women for a long time, and I find them particularly interesting, but as soon as I see them wearing the most modern high-heeled shoes, but still walking with a splayed gait, I can't help but sigh that although people are modern, they still carry some ancient Chinese style!

All night long, I smelled the smell of opium smoke and the sound of mahjong. In such a sleepless night, I can't help but think of the different styles of smoking opium. For example, Lao Chen, who is from our hometown, is a plasterer. His opium pipe and lamp are always ready. As long as he has time, he can lie under the shade of a tree or in a quiet place in a dark alley and smoke a few puffs casually. This is one style. There is also the old scholar in our hometown who teaches "Confucius said." In addition to teaching, he is always lying on a couch all day long, with the oil lamp as small as a bean, smoking slowly and delicately. After smoking enough opium, he raises his hand, raises his foot, stretches his voice, and talks at length about ancient and modern times, and then shakes his pen and writes out famous sentences such as "Closing the door and shutting the household, covering the thatched fence." These two styles of smoking opium can probably be said to be romantic or classical. As for the middle-aged man with a handlebar mustache who lives next door to me, he is lying under the pale green light and on a "cubist" wooden bed to smoke opium.

This style of smoking is the first time I have seen it in my life. I think this can probably be said to be realistic or modern!

Stinky Tofu

— Wei Zhen

"Stinky tofu! Three copper coins for two pieces!" A crisp and audible call, along with an indescribable fragrance, spread around an alley. The sister-in-law in the pavilion on the second floor, the mother of Ah Gou in the pavilion on the third floor, the wife in the front room, the young lady in the back room, the apron aunt... like flies seeing sugar, they gathered naturally with warbling voices, surrounding this load of stinky tofu so tightly that no water could leak through. You buy four pieces, I buy six pieces, so that the one who combines several positions - shareholder, manager, and salesperson - the fried tofu vendor is so busy that he can't handle it, tearing open his golden-toothed oily mouth that can't close, drool adding fragrance to the tofu, constantly spraying...

Praising the fragrance when buying flowers is people's habit. No one wants to add ugly nouns to their own goods. However, the one who sells stinky tofu not only doesn't praise his own goods as the best, but also loudly tells people that it is stinky. I think: The most honest people in the world are only them! Originally, their business could not be done, no, the facts tell me that many people flock to it! It can be seen that, whether it is a thing or a person, there is no need for people's praise and ridicule, only the actual and true flavor of itself, and there is no need to be afraid of being abandoned by society! Stinky tofu can give us good evidence.

The Last Night at the Jai Alai Palace

— Yun Chi

Here, you can find two different kinds of gamblers: one is the bourgeoisie who have no other way to kill time, and the other is the unemployed masses who have absolutely no way out. The former only uses money as a game, while the latter stakes their lives. Those who use money as a game often win money, while those who stake their lives are certain to lose their lives.

Lukov has not been himself since he started gambling on jai alai: his eyes bulge, his cheeks are sunken, and his grayish-yellow complexion is like that of a chronic lung disease patient. In his heart, he also knows that this is a last resort. However, because he cherishes life so much, he does not hesitate to use his life as a stake: if he doesn't gamble, he knows he will commit suicide in the future; if he gambles, maybe he will have a chance to turn things around. Thus, he became a seeker of disillusionment day and night.

Borrowing and pawning methods have been exhausted, and even the idea of stealing sometimes flickers in his mind. "When life comes to an end, what else is there to be afraid of doing!" He often thinks like this. But, he still doesn't have that kind of courage after all.

Today is Lukov's last night to go to the Jai Alai Palace. From borrowing and pawning everywhere, he scraped together twenty dollars. In the eyes of others, this meager amount is nothing. But he thinks of it as the price of life. If he wins, he can still eke out a living; if he loses, the whole family will perish together.

He prayed to God, bid farewell to his wife, mustered his courage, and went straight to the dazzling neon lights of Avenue Albert, as solemn as if heading to the battlefield.

He sat alone in a corner, intently watching the movements of the entire team of players. The images of six first-tier players, Lamos, Shatelanggu, Erga, Albati, Cuban Dragon, and Houlando, swirled in his mind.

Lukov watched several games before deciding to stake the twenty dollars on Erga. This is the twelfth game, and Erga is placed in number six. "The rest are all favorites, even if they win, you won't win much money. Only Erga's number six is really cold. If he wins, a ten-dollar ticket will be worth at least one hundred dollars. And Erga is playing well today, so let's risk life on it!" After thinking this, his feet involuntarily walked to the place to buy tickets.

With trembling hands, he took out two ten-dollar bills from his pocket and exchanged them for two red and green pieces of paper.

The bell ended, and two referees walked out from inside. When Lukov saw them, he felt as if they were executioners killing him. Suddenly, there was a silver whistle, the whole place was silent, and even the radio stopped singing obediently.

Lukov stood in front of the wire fence, his heart pounding.

His hot blood surged with the sound of the ball, and his eyes followed the players. Suddenly, it was Erga's turn to play. He mustered up more courage and shouted loudly at the wire fence:

Come on Acha, Come on Acha!

Sure enough, Erga won a point. At this time, a red color appeared on his face. He clapped his hands as hard as he could, shaking the entire stadium. Because his life was in Erga's hands. However, there were also many people making "boo" sounds, because Erga was an underdog, and most of the gamblers didn't want him to win.

However, Erga finally lived up to expectations, and in the midst of "boo" and "clap," he won another point. At this time, Lukov cheered even more vigorously:

Come on Acha! Come on Acha!!

Lukov used all his strength in his hands and feet. If there were no wire fence blocking him, maybe he would rush into the stadium to help Erga.

Erga scored four points in a row. When Lukov saw this, his heart was about to jump out of his mouth. He clapped his hands desperately again. Although his hands were sore from clapping, he still didn't feel it. Come on Acha!!! One more!!!

He cheered at Erga like this. If he scored one more point, his life could be preserved.

At this time, Erga was playing against Lamos. Lukov had already been wary, because he knew that Erga could not beat Lamos.

His face was red and white for a while. Who knew that when Erga served the ball, he hit it into the first red line.

"Mala!" The referee raised his hand and shouted this. This "Mala" sound was like a bullet hitting his chest. Then Lukov's face changed from white to green, and from green to gray.

However, others only had one or two points, and Erga already had four points, so this game was not over yet. Erga still had a chance.

Now Lamos is playing against Shatelanggu. Who knew that Shatelanggu defeated four players in a row, so he also got four points. Then it was Erga's turn again. This is four points against four points, success or failure depends on this move, who knows who will win.

Lukov's life was in this instant. He didn't dare to look up again. He was about to faint in front of the wire fence.

In an instant, he suddenly heard a silver whistle and thunderous applause. He knew that something was not good. Looking at the score on the scoreboard, sure enough, Shatelanggu won. Erga only had four points, useless.

He stood there blankly, almost unable to support his body. The melodious radio music served as his elegy, sending him out the door.

The next morning, the local news in various newspapers published a message about an unidentified man throwing himself into the river. No family members were found. The Pushan Villa was ordered to provide a coffin to bury the body.

Lu Zishu is Known by His Style Name, a Person from Guangdong

Amateur Mailbox: Self-Study That Takes Into Account Writing and Reading

Editor Sir;

Since leaving school and entering society, I have fortunately found a place to eat in a factory. Although the work is hard, compared to my unemployed friends, I am still lucky. The work here is twelve hours a day 丨丨 from six in the morning to six in the evening 丨丨 after work, I have to wash my own clothes and tidy up the dormitory. If you want to write a word after finishing your work, it is already late, and if you don't sleep, you won't be able to get up tomorrow! Therefore, there is no way to do anything in your spare time! Our "spare time" is basically non-existent!

However, the fear of knowledge is a feeling shared by every young person, especially our group of dropouts, who feel the need even more urgently. I really hope everyone will study, but few of my colleagues are in the same mood as me, because they are all burdened with families and wives. So, I am alone.

Although the factory has subscribed to two daily newspapers (Shen Bao and Xinwen Bao), you are not allowed to read them as much as you want during working hours: the environment is like this, making it really impossible to think. However, in any case, I am very interested in literature and art. In the supplements, I saw many moving and great works, which made me admire and ashamed. I always have the question, "We are all young people, why am I so useless?" I often sell and encourage myself like this, but how can one make progress by groping in the dark? Therefore, I turned my attention to the library and writing articles. Everyone knows that the library is the best place to increase knowledge. What about submitting articles? It can also arouse the interest in writing works. Therefore, I have two questions, and I am sorry to ask you for instructions. Of course, sir, you will definitely not have so much free time, but here I sincerely request you, in any case, give me a reply, the sooner or later the time does not matter. I want to ask, is it possible to submit articles to the supplement? Am I good enough? How should the manuscript paper be written? What is the procedure for submitting articles? Also, regarding the library, it is said that the circulating library attached to your newspaper requires a deposit of two yuan for borrowing books, and readers of Shen Bao only need one yuan. I wonder if I can be considered a reader of Shen Bao? Can I get preferential treatment? If so, what do I need to prove it? (Because the newspaper in the factory is subscribed to from newspaper vendors.) These are two very ridiculous questions, and I am troubling you heavily 丨 I wish you good health Wang Yuanxing respectfully

X X X X X

Editor's note: It is truly commendable that Mr. Wang can still not forget to seek to increase his knowledge after extremely busy work. The circulating library attached to this newspaper is purely for the purpose of serving society, and everything is free of charge. However, in order to ensure that the borrowed books are not lost for no reason, there is a regulation that each reader needs to pay a deposit. In the future, any reader who withdraws due to any reason will have the deposit returned in full. According to your situation, if you can show the receipt from the newspaper vendor, you can also receive preferential treatment according to the qualifications of a reader of this newspaper, and only pay one yuan. In addition, if you find it inconvenient to travel back and forth due to the distance, then as long as you come to the library in person once for the first time, you can follow the postal borrowing method in the future, and the postage for sending the books to you will also be borne by the library. As for the matter of submitting articles, it is also worth a try. The supplements of this newspaper and other newspapers mostly welcome submissions. The procedure for submitting articles is also very simple, just add new-style punctuation to the manuscript and send it directly to each newspaper, and write the words XX supplement on the envelope. Recently, the literary platform has been paying attention to the description of real life, and is not as strict on literary and artistic aspects as before. People with such rich lives, if they can use the spirit of creation to write articles, have a very promising future. However, each publication has its own stance, and you must understand it carefully. The same article, if it is not published in X publication, may be welcomed by other supplements at the same time. This point must be noted, otherwise the editor, with his iron face and impartiality, will inevitably give you a disappointment.

Yan Zhu's "Tragedy in Loneliness" Published Young writer Yan Chonglou, has recently used the once sensational box corpse case materials, to write a collection of long novels, "Tragedy in Loneliness", the book for modern young men and women caught in the bitter love of the situation, described vividly, and for those sacrificed under the environment, especially deep sympathy, the whole book ten thousand words, with Daolin paper fine printing, the beginning of the article has Zheng Boqi long preface, and attached art illustrations, each book only sells three corners, modern, Kai Ming major bookstores, are available, heard that the first edition of one thousand copies, is about to be sold out cloud,

Notice on February 30th, a certain school in this newspaper's local supplement, Shao Lin, is purely a fictional fact and should be corrected.

Novel

Shanghai (20)

— Zhang Lao San

31 Medical Expenses

A question came to my mind. I had been sick for two months. When I was seriously ill, I was unconscious and didn't know anything. Seeing a doctor and taking medicine, I thought that all the expenses would be a shocking amount. No one in the club could afford it. Like me, they couldn't dream of having stacks of banknotes in their pockets except for this body that could be exchanged for money. At this time, I saw my younger brother take out a silver coin. I wanted to know what was going on, or if I had harmed many friends. A sentence was surging in my throat, but my sister signaled to me with her eyes, and changed the direction of the conversation.

"Brother, I'll take you to a restaurant tonight." She stroked her brother's head and laughed at Sister Hui.

Sister Hui snatched the younger brother's hand and hugged him in her arms, saying:

"I'll take you to see a dance."

A burst of laughter swept away this doubt.

My body gradually recovered. I slowly browsed through some foreign manuscripts. Sister Hui came to the club every night. She said that she had become interested in literature and art, and brought short poems and short pieces of writing. Although they were not necessarily masterpieces, I was very happy that a city girl could suddenly change her usual state and devote herself to this kind of trick of literature and art. She also mentioned that a drama club had recently been organized in the school, and she seemed to regret that she had missed an opportunity to perform because she had not been to school for more than a month.

"Oh, you haven't been to school for more than a month. Is there anything going on at home?" I didn't take my eyes off my paper and pen. I was overly sensitive for a moment, thinking that something unexpected had happened to my uncle, so my tone of voice was very panicked.

Sister Min stumbled and said:

"When you were sick, she was by your bed every day. Didn't you see her?"

The friends in the living room all laughed, and I laughed along with them; however, the question of medical expenses floated in my memory again. I still haven't figured out who helped me with this big favor, and there is no suitable opportunity or suitable person to solve this mystery for me.

That night, I used the excuse of taking a walk to pull Gao Fei out, and mentioned this question intentionally or unintentionally.

"Gao Fei, I didn't expect to be so seriously ill."

"You take everything too seriously. I think you should change this old temper." He squinted his eyes and stretched his hands upwards, his words like William Heis's comedic posture "I'm afraid later..."

"Stop talking nonsense." I interrupted him "I don't know how much debt this medical expense has put me in?"
